## 0. Build philosophy (north star)

StructureBot is built to persist. A failing result is a diagnostic signal, not a verdict. The default response to a shortcoming is to root-cause and solve it вЂ” not to work around it, lower the bar, or write off a component. "It can't be done" is a conclusion that must be earned through investigation, never assumed. Honest assessment exists to direct the fix, not to justify stopping; a caveat flags a real risk to be solved, it is not an exit. Precedent: an apparent 47% "weak local model" was a silent num_ctx truncation throttle, found only because the first verdict was refused and the config audited.

### Named build rule вЂ” Intent/Render separation

**"The LLM infers and clarifies intent; it never writes tool syntax."**

For any operation class where the set of valid outputs is known and finite, the LLM returns a canonical INTENT LABEL from a closed vocabulary вЂ” it never emits the tool-specific syntax directly. A separate deterministic render layer owns the syntax (single source of truth, probe-verified). This decoupling means: (a) miscategorization is recoverable via the 3-tier resolution pipeline (alias в†’ LLM classifier в†’ graceful miss), (b) malformed syntax for covered ops is structurally impossible, (c) the LLM's role stays what it is good at вЂ” understanding natural language вЂ” not what it is bad at (memorizing exact API calling conventions).

**3-tier resolution pipeline:** (1) Deterministic alias match (substring, instant, no LLM); (2) LLM constrained classifier (`make_llm_classify_fn()` вЂ” returns ONLY a label from the valid set, "uncovered", or "none"; never prose or syntax); (3) Graceful miss (lists the known intents, asks the user to rephrase вЂ” never guesses). Tier 1 covers the common phrases; Tier 2 handles paraphrases; Tier 3 ensures the system never silently does the wrong thing.

**LLM classifier backend (2026-06-08 fix):** the classifier calls the SAME configured backend as the translator (Ollama when Claude is capped), and always falls back to Ollama on any primary failure. The Ollama call places `think: false` at the **TOP LEVEL** of the request JSON вЂ” NOT inside `options{}`. For qwen3 models, `think` inside `options` is silently ignored and the model generates a thinking block that consumes `num_predict` tokens в†’ empty response в†’ classified as miss. With the fix, `num_predict` is 60 (not 30) to avoid truncation on longer intent keys. The Claude API monthly cap no longer kills the classification tier.

**Per-target representation snapshot + undo intent (2026-06-08):** before executing any non-undo render, `ToolRouter._snapshot_repr()` probes the current atoms/cartoon/style state via `runscript` and stores restore commands in `_repr_snapshots[spec]`. `view.undo_representation` intent ("strip it back", "undo that", "put it back", etc.) executes the stored restore commands and clears the snapshot. No prior snapshot в†’ graceful miss (not a free-translation guess).

**Noun-floor gate + authoritative alias (2026-06-08 structural fix; surface tier revised same day вЂ” FIX 2):** `detect_category_phrase()` now uses two structural tiers instead of a literal-phrase list. (1a) Authoritative alias match вЂ” `resolve_alias()` positive в†’ always representation (catches "strip it back", "undo that", etc. regardless of other words in the phrase). The old phrase-list veto (`_REP_SURFACE_NEGATIVE`) is **removed**; "surface" no longer resolves via a bare alias, so there is nothing to veto. (1b) Conservative noun-floor вЂ” unambiguous rep nouns (cartoon, ribbon, spacefill, stick/sticks, ball/balls, wire/wireframe, mesh, licorice, cpk) are always flagged; ambiguous nouns вЂ” atom/atoms, sphere/spheres, **and now surface/surfaces** вЂ” flag ONLY when a display verb is also present (one shared verb set: show, hide, remove, display, style, reveal, add, apply, ditch, lose, drop, "get rid of", "no more"). Bare-token "surface"/"surfaces" as the whole input в†’ treated as rep. Single-word verbs are matched on word boundaries (`\bвЂ¦\b`) so "drop" inside "hydrophobic" and "lose" inside "closely" do NOT false-fire; multi-word verbs ("get rid of") substring-match safely. This is structural вЂ” "lose the sticks", "get rid of the balls on chain A", "ditch the surface", "show the surface" are caught deterministically; "fold the top design", "how many atoms", "binding surface", "the surface of the dimer", "hydrophobic surface patch", "surface contacts between chains" are NOT over-blocked (they free-translate to a biology/render answer instead of silently no-op'ing as they did under the old veto).

**Emission guard at execution choke-point (В§0 invariant; origin-scoped вЂ” FIX 1, 2026-06-08):** `main._execute_commands(commands, origin=...)` runs an emission guard before calling `bridge.run_commands()`. The guard fires **only for `origin="translation"`** (the default вЂ” free-translated commands from the translator/error-fix path). Any representation-shaped command (hide/show with #spec and atoms/cartoons/sphere/surface targets; style #spec sphere/stick/ball; surface/~surface #spec; bare cartoon/ribbon/spacefill with #spec) from translation is **blocked with an error** вЂ” it never reaches ChimeraX. Three execution paths, three trust levels: (a) the **render layer** (`_run_representation()`) bypasses `_execute_commands()` entirely; (b) **tool-generated viz** (ColabFold cartoon, double-mutant cartoon/show/style/label/distance) calls `_execute_commands(viz_cmds, origin="tool_viz")` вЂ” a trusted origin that is guard-exempt; (c) **free-translation** (`origin="translation"`) is the only guarded origin. The structural invariant holds: even if the category gate misses a phrase and the translator emits a representation command, it cannot execute вЂ” while legitimate tool viz is never falsely blocked. Note this is an **origin** parameter, not a `skip_guard=True` bypass switch вЂ” a tool cannot opt OUT of guarding; it declares WHAT it is, and the guard policy is owned centrally. Live-confirmed 2026-06-08: double-mutant scan ran 43 viz commands / 0 blocked; free-translated `cartoon #1` (from "binding surface") blocked as expected.

**Pre-translate interception:** covered operations bypass `translate()` entirely вЂ” `detect_category_phrase()` in `_handle_request()` routes to the representation tool before the translator is called, avoiding both the latency and the risk of the LLM writing syntax for a covered op.

**Post-command verify guard:** after executing render-layer commands, `_probe_atom_count()` (via `runscript`) confirms the structural state changed as expected. A False verify is a warning; a None verify (probe failed) is a safe no-op.

**Error detection hardening:** `_ERROR_PREFIXES` in `chimerax_bridge.py` now includes `"Expected"` to catch `"Expected a collection of one of 'atoms', 'bonds'вЂ¦"` вЂ” previously these were silently passed as success. Any response matching an error prefix is `FAILED`, not `вњ“`.

**Current scope:** viewer representation intents (cartoon/spacefill/sticks/ball-and-stick/surface/hide-atoms/hide-cartoon/hide-surface/show-atoms/undo-representation). Operation-class migration (color, selection, etc.) is the documented next phase вЂ” see В§9.

---

## 1. Project Overview

StructureBot is a Windows-native natural-language interface for UCSF ChimeraX 1.11.1, running on Python 3.14 (main venv) with a GPU/ML delegation layer in Python 3.12 (venv312). Users type free-text biology requests ("suggest mutations to improve solubility of chain A, avoiding interfaces") into a Rich-console REPL; the system translates those requests via the Anthropic Claude API (claude-sonnet-4-6 with prompt caching), routes them through a pipeline of computational bridges (CamSol, ESM-2, ProteinMPNN, PyRosetta, DynaMut2, disulfide/proline/glycan/cavity/salt-bridge/double-mutant analysers), and executes the resulting ChimeraX commands via the ChimeraX REST API on port 60001. The application also supports a `--script` batch mode and session persistence via `session.json`.

---

## 2. Architecture

### Data Flow

```
User input (Rich REPL or --script file)
  в”‚
  в–ј
main.py / StructureBot
  в”‚  1. config.load_env_file()  в†ђ loads .env.local FIRST
  в”‚  2. CommandTranslator.translate()
  в”‚     в””в”Ђ Anthropic API (claude-sonnet-4-6)
  в”‚        Block 1: STATIC prompt (cached, ephemeral cache_control)
  в”‚        Block 2: DYNAMIC session context (uncached, changes per turn)
  в”‚  3. ToolRouter.route()      в†ђ augments result, no execution
  в”‚     Intent overrides (in order): validate_ddg в†’ colabfold в†’ proline в†’ mpnn_esmfold
  в”‚     в†’ glycan_positions в†’ netnglyc в†’ glycan в†’ salt_bridge в†’ cavity в†’ double_mutant
  в”‚     в†’ mutation_scan (fallback, last)
  в”‚  4. User confirmation / auto-proceed countdown
  в”‚  5. ChimeraXBridge.run_commands()  в†ђ initial viz commands
  в”‚  6. ToolRouter.execute()    в†ђ computational pipeline
  в”‚     в”њв”Ђ CamsolBridge         в†ђ local algorithm, no network
  в”‚     в”њв”Ђ EsmBridge            в†ђ delegates to venv312 subprocess
  в”‚     в”њв”Ђ ESMFoldBridge        в†ђ delegates to venv312 subprocess
  в”‚     в”њв”Ђ RosettaBridge        в†ђ DynaMut2 API or WSL2 PyRosetta
  в”‚     в”њв”Ђ MutationScanner      в†ђ orchestrates CamSol+ESM+Rosetta
  в”‚     в”њв”Ђ DoubleMutantBridge   в†ђ DynaMut2 prediction_mm + optional PyRosetta
  в”‚     в”њв”Ђ DisulfideBridge      в†ђ BioPython + ESM + DynaMut2
  в”‚     в”њв”Ђ ProlineBridge        в†ђ BioPython + ESM
  в”‚     в”њв”Ђ GlycanBridge         в†ђ BioPython + ESM + NetNGlyc API
  в”‚     в”њв”Ђ AssemblyAnalyser     в†ђ RCSB API + ChimeraX zone-select
  в”‚     в”њв”Ђ SaltBridgeBridge     в†ђ BioPython + FreeSASA
  в”‚     в”њв”Ђ CavityBridge         в†ђ BioPython ShrakeRupley
  в”‚     в”њв”Ђ ProteinMPNNBridge    в†ђ subprocess: protein_mpnn_run.py
  в”‚     в”њв”Ђ ColabFoldBridge      в†ђ WSL2 ~/colabfold_env worker (AF2, remote MSA)
  в”‚     в””в”Ђ RFdiffusionBridge    в†ђ SCAFFOLD (wsl.exeв†’RFDIFFUSION_PYTHON; not activated)
  в”‚  7. ChimeraXBridge.run_commands()  в†ђ viz commands from tools
  в”‚  8. SessionState.add_to_history()
  в”‚
  в–ј
ChimeraX REST API  (http://127.0.0.1:60001/run)
```

### Two-Venv Architecture

| Venv | Python | Purpose |
|------|--------|---------|
| `venv/` | 3.14 | Main process: Anthropic SDK, Rich, BioPython, requests, all bridges |
| `venv312/` | 3.12 | GPU/ML delegation: torch 2.11.0+cu128 (RTX 5070 Ti, sm_120), ESM-2 inference, ESMFold inference |

The main venv cannot run GPU inference because no PyTorch cu128 build exists for Python 3.14. ESM-related bridges spawn `venv312/Scripts/python.exe` as a subprocess with JSON I/O (`--input`, `--output` temp files). Worker scripts have **no project imports** вЂ” they only import `torch`, `transformers`, `esm`, and stdlib.

### WSL2 Layer (PyRosetta)

When `ROSETTA_BACKEND=local`, `RosettaBridge._run_rosetta_local()` builds a standalone Python worker script as an f-string, writes it to a Windows temp file, translates the path to `/mnt/c/...` form, and runs it via `WSLBridge.run_python_script()` в†’ `wsl.exe --distribution Ubuntu-24.04 --exec bash -c "{PYROSETTA_PYTHON} '{wsl_path}'"`. Results are returned as a JSON file at `/tmp/rosetta_ddg_{hash}.json`, copied back to Windows via `wsl.exe`. Same pattern applies to `DoubleMutantBridge._run_pair_pyrosetta()` for close pairs.

**Worker script constraints** (critical, applies to ALL worker scripts):
- No project imports вЂ” completely standalone
- Communicates only via JSON files in `/tmp/`
- All subprocess calls in `wsl_bridge.py` use `stdin=subprocess.DEVNULL` and `creationflags=subprocess.CREATE_NO_WINDOW`

Calls the configured backend (Claudeв†’Ollama fallback on any failure including usage cap). Ollama call places `think: false` at TOP LEVEL (not inside `options{}`); `num_predict=60`. Returns a valid intent key, "uncovered" (representation-category but no specific match в†’ graceful miss), or "none" (not a representation request в†’ graceful miss) вЂ” NEVER syntax. `_CATEGORY_TRIGGERS["view"]` вЂ” broader trigger phrases for pre-translate interception (2026-06-08: expanded with `"all spheres"`, `"all atoms"`, and undo triggers `"strip it back"`, `"undo that"`, `"put it back"`, etc.); `view.hide_atoms` (`hide {spec} atoms` вЂ” NOT `hide {spec} sphere`); `view.hide_cartoon` (`hide {spec} cartoons`); `view.hide_surface` (`~surface {spec}`); `view.show_atoms` (`show {spec} atoms`); **`view.undo_representation`** (aliases: "strip it back", "undo that", "put it back", etc.; render_fn returns [] вЂ” execution handled specially in `_run_representation()`). **Verify guards** use pattern `(lambda n: None if n is None else (n == 0))(probe_result)` so a failed probe (n=None) is a safe None, not False. **`tool_router._run_representation()`** is the integration point: does the 3-tier resolution, snapshots before rendering, executes render-layer commands via bridge, handles undo, runs verify, returns `ToolStepResult`. **`main.py` pre-translate interception:** `detect_category_phrase()` check fires before `translate()`, so covered ops never reach the translator. **`chimerax_bridge._ERROR_PREFIXES`** extended with `"Expected"` to catch `"Expected a collection of one of 'atoms', 'bonds'вЂ¦"`. 109 tests in `tests/test_intent_registry.py`. **COLOR op-class (2026-06-09, Priority 0.5 вЂ” SECOND op-class on this framework):** `COLOR_REGISTRY` = `IntentRegistry` with 6 color intents, syntax probe-verified spec-FIRST against ChimeraX 1.11.1: `color.by_chain` (`color {spec} bychain`), `color.by_element` (`color {spec} byelement`), `color.by_heteroatom` (`color {spec} byhetero`), `color.rainbow` (`rainbow {spec}`), `color.by_attribute` (`color byattribute bfactor {spec} palette blue:white:red` вЂ” bfactor ONLY; hydrophobicity is not a built-in attr), `color.solid` (`color {spec} {named}`, resolved via `extract_named_color()` not alias). **Conservative gate** `_color_category_floor()`: requires an explicit color verb (`color/colour/recolor/вЂ¦`) or `rainbow` AND no sub-chain selection qualifier (`_COLOR_COMPLEX_RE`: residue type/range, named region, property) вЂ” so "color the proline residues" / "color the binding pocket" fall through to free-translation (the op-class targets only a whole chain or whole model). `detect_category_phrase(text, "color")` gates on the floor ONLY (color scheme aliases like "by chain"/"bfactor" are common non-color substrings в†’ NOT treated as authoritative, unlike viewer). `make_llm_classify_fn(registry=, task_block=)` generalised (viewer default unchanged; `_COLOR_TASK_BLOCK` for color). **`tool_router._run_color()`** is the integration point вЂ” parses target (whole chain / whole model; "each/every/all chain" в†’ whole model), resolves scheme-alias в†’ solid(named color) в†’ LLM в†’ graceful miss, renders, then reuses `translator._scope_chain_refs_to_macromolecule` so chain colors never bleed onto ligand/solvent/ions (the payoff bug). **Emission-guard extension to color DEFERRED** (false-block risk; tools emit `color bychain` in viz). Color undo DEFERRED. 66 tests in `tests/test_color_intent.py` (incl. real-`main._handle_request` integration). Live-verified on 1HSG: `color chain A red` в†’ `color (#1/A & ~ligand & ~solvent & ~ions) red`, probe solvent_red=0/ligand_red=0; paraphrase в†’ resolution=llm (Ollama). |
| `main.py` | `StructureBot`, `_ElapsedTicker`, `_maybe_restore_session()`, `_reconnect_or_offer_reopen()`, `_cmd_clear_session()` | вњ… Complete | REPL + `--script` mode; startup sequence. **Session auto-restore on startup**: offers to restore a previous `session.json` (restore / keep / delete), then checks whether each restored structure is still in ChimeraX and offers a fast re-open if not; `clear session` / `new session` command wipes `session.json` and resets state. Script mode skips restore prompts (`_interactive=False`). **AU-vs-biological mismatch detector (2026-06-07, Component 2):** `_display_assembly_type_on_open` now compares `n_subunits` from RCSB assembly metadata against `_model_chains` count; if biological > loaded в†’ yellow advisory ("Loaded the asymmetric unit (N chains); biological assembly is a {type} вЂ” generate it with 'work as {type}'?"); informational only, not auto-applied; silently suppressed on any exception (never blocks the open). **Correction-loop same-verb halt (2026-06-07, Component 3b):** `_handle_request` extracts the leading verb of `failed_cmd` and `fix_cmds[0]`; if they match AND the verb is not in the safe standard set (`open`, `close`, `color`, `sym`, `matchmaker`, вЂ¦) в†’ halt with "Correction re-proposed the same non-existent verb вЂ” halting to prevent a loop" instead of looping endlessly on a hallucinated verb. |
| `config.py` | constants + `load_env_file()` | вњ… Complete | Called first in `main.py`; all env-var overrides centralised here. **`TRANSLATOR_TOOL_NAMES` now 24 entries** (added `"interface_stabilization"` 2026-06-07; was 23 after `"bio_assembly"` added 2026-06-07) вЂ” the ENUM constraint for Ollama schema-constrained JSON and the `TOOL_REGISTRY` source in `eval_harness.py`. **`INTERFACE_COLOR_BY_CHAIN` (2026-06-07):** bool, default True; enables sub-model-aware 4-color chain coloring in `_build_viz_commands`. Set to false to skip recoloring and preserve user-set colors. |
| `translator.py` | `CommandTranslator`, `TranslatorBackend`, `ClaudeBackend`, `OllamaBackend`, `make_backend()`, `ensure_translator_unloaded()`, `TRANSLATION_JSON_SCHEMA` | вњ… Complete | NLв†’ChimeraX translation via a **pluggable LLM backend** (`config.TRANSLATOR_BACKEND`, `"claude"` default / `"ollama"`). `TranslatorBackend.translate(translator, user_input, session)` returns the normalized 7-key translation dict; `ClaudeBackend` wraps the Anthropic-API logic verbatim, reusing the translator's **single shared prompt** (`_build_system_blocks` / `_static_block`) + primitives (`_pre_screen`/`_call_api`/`_parse_response`). **`OllamaBackend`** (local; benchmark + fallback role) reuses the SAME prompt + `_parse_response`, emitting **schema-constrained JSON** via Ollama `/api/chat` `format=TRANSLATION_JSON_SCHEMA` (NOT tool-calls), `temperature=0`, `keep_alive`. **`tools_needed` is ENUM-constrained** to `config.TRANSLATOR_TOOL_NAMES` (the router registry) so the model can't emit a misspelled/hallucinated/wrong-cased tool; plus a **targeted few-shot** (local-backend only; `translator_corpus.few_shot_messages`, sourced from the disjoint EXAMPLE_POOL) вЂ” **FEW_SHOT_POOL_V2**: 17 pairs / 15 execute В· 1 clarify В· 1 refuse, teaching the measured weak spots (camsol/mpnn/esm routing, argument-shape `design_positions`, zone chain-direction, prolineв†’mutation_scan, inferential T2, plus clarify/refuse balance) AND three V2 **mutation_scan boundary contrasts** (esm tolerance / proteinmpnn negation-redesign / camsol+esm compound route away from mutation_scan, correcting the V1 over-attraction). (Critically, `OLLAMA_NUM_CTX` was raised to 16384 вЂ” the ~7.5k-token prompt + few-shot was being silently truncated at 8192, which was the dominant cause of the routing collapse.) `CommandTranslator.translate` delegates to the configured backend then applies the **backend-agnostic** deterministic guards вЂ” identical for both: (1) `_sanitize_zone_syntax` (Chimera-1 `zone`в†’`:<`), then (2) **`_scope_chain_refs_to_macromolecule`** вЂ” a "chain X" reference must target ONLY that chain's macromolecule, never a ligand/solvent/ion sharing the chain id (the 1HSG MK1=B:902 bleed where "colour chain B red" reddened the ligand too). Every BARE chain selector `(#N)?/X` is wrapped `(вЂ¦ & ~ligand & ~solvent & ~ions)` (keeps any polymer в†’ nucleic-safe); the `ligand` keyword and explicit residue/atom sub-refs (`/B:902`, `/B@CA`), negations (`~/B`) and file paths are left untouched, so chainв‡„ligand stay DISJOINT across ALL operations (color/hide/show/select/zone refs). **One-directional fallback** (`_translate_via_backend`): active=claude + a real Claude API failure (`_CLAUDE_FALLBACK_ERRORS`: connection/timeout/auth/rate-limit, **OR a usage/spend-cap `BadRequestError`** вЂ” a 400 `invalid_request_error` whose message reports a usage limit, matched NARROWLY by `is_usage_cap_error` so a genuinely malformed 400 still surfaces) + `TRANSLATOR_FALLBACK` в†’ fall back to Ollama (`_may_fall_back`/`_fall_back_to_ollama`); a refusal/imperfect response is NOT a trigger; forced `"ollama"` NEVER falls back. **Per-session Claude usage-cap latch (`_claude_capped`, 2026-06-09, Priority 0.4):** once a usage/spend-cap rejection is seen and we fall back, `_translate_via_backend` latches and routes every subsequent translate straight to Ollama (only when `_may_fall_back()`) вЂ” eliminating the wasted capped Claude round-trip per uncovered op. Routes directly (not via `_fall_back_to_ollama`) since ClaudeBackend was never called that turn, so there is no dangling user turn to pop. Latches ONLY on the durable cap; a transient connection/timeout still falls back per-call WITHOUT latching (a blip must not disable Claude for the session). Mirrors the intent classifier's latch. **Backstop:** `main._handle_request` also catches any non-refusal translate() error (`_report_translation_error`) so a usage-cap with fallback OFF surfaces cleanly instead of crashing the REPL. **`ensure_translator_unloaded()`** frees the local model from VRAM (`keep_alive=0`) вЂ” called by `tool_router._dispatch_tool` BEFORE any `_GPU_BRIDGE_TOOLS` run; cheap/idempotent; no-op under Claude. Prompt caching; rolling history `MAX_CONVERSATION_HISTORY=6`. **3a registry/allowlist fix (2026-06-07):** **Root cause**: `probe_chimerax_verbs()` was defined but NEVER called in production (`main.py`/`tool_router.py`/`chimerax_bridge.py`), so `_chimerax_verb_registry` was always `None` at translation time and Tier 2 never fired вЂ” only the denylist protected, and `assembly_analyser` wasn't in it. **Fix**: (1) `probe_chimerax_verbs(self.bridge.run_command)` wired into `main._handle_request` BEFORE `translate()` is called (idempotent вЂ” only probes once per session); (2) `_HALLUCINATED_VERB_DENYLIST` cleaned back to the original 10 common-English-word entries (`find`/`search`/`locate`/`lookup`/`retrieve`/`fetch_sequence`/`query`/`get_sequence`/`list_structures`/`display_structure`) вЂ” StructureBot tool names removed (they're the registry's job, not an enumerated list). Now Tier 2 GENERALISES: `assembly_analyser`, `bio_assembly`, `tetramer_builder`, or any other non-ChimeraX verb is caught automatically without being enumerated. `sym #1 assembly 1 copies true` passes (192-entry 1.11.1 registry contains `sym`). **Live confirmed (2VNC, 2026-06-07)**: `assembly_analyser` NOT in denylist AND NOT in registry в†’ blocked via Tier 2; `tetramer_builder`, `fold_protein`, `analyse_complex` (all novel, not enumerated) в†’ also blocked via Tier 2; `open`/`color`/`matchmaker`/`transparency`/`close`/`sym` в†’ all pass |

See В§4 config rows. 4 backends (dynamut2/empirical/pyrosetta-stub/local-WSL2). **DynaMut2 single parser fixed** вЂ” handles current status-based API (`status` DONE/RUNNING/ERROR), robust float cast of `prediction`, raises (never silent 0.0) on ERROR. **Local PyRosetta path hardened**: `pose_from_file` validation + `.pdb`-extension/`pose_from_pdb` fallback; whole-batch failure в†’ per-mutation **empirical fallback** (not all-zero); each value carries **`ddg_source`** (`pyrosetta`/`empirical`). **Tiered multi-trajectory ddG**: `_run_rosetta_local(num_trajectories=, relax_cycles=)` runs N independent relax+score trajectories per mutation (per-trajectory RNG seed when N>1), aggregates by **median** (`_aggregate_ddg_trajectories`), reports **MAD spread** + **`ddg_confidence`** (`_ddg_confidence_label`); WSL timeout scales by NГ—cycles. | `mutation_scanner.py` | `MutationScanner`, `combined_score()`, `effective_weights()` | вњ… Complete (tiered + scoped 2026-06-09) | CamSol+ESM+Rosetta pipeline; deep-tier combined score `0.5Г—(-ddG) + 0.3Г—camsol_delta + 0.2Г—esm_tolerance`; Pro/Cys exclusion; interface protection. `_run_rosetta_batch` returns `(ddg_scores, ddg_source, ddg_spread, ddg_confidence)`; spread/confidence threaded into scan results + the summary table (scans are single-trajectory в†’ confidence "single-trajectory"). **Triageв†’validate tiering (Priority 1, 2026-06-09):** `scan()` gains `run_rosetta: bool` + `include_positions: Optional[List[int]]`. **Fast/default tier (`run_rosetta=False`)** = CamSol + ESM only вЂ” **`_run_rosetta_batch` (the only WSL2/PyRosetta spawn) is NOT called**; ddG is reported as `None` ("not computed (opt in with 'rosetta')") вЂ” **never a fake 0.0** вЂ” and the score is **renormalised** by `effective_weights(use_ddg=False)` (drops `_W_DDG=0.50`, rescales `0.30/0.20 в†’ 0.6/0.4`; structured so ThermoMPNN/RaSP can join the fast tier with another renormalise). **Deep tier (`run_rosetta=True`)** runs the existing Rosetta path. **Assignable scope (`include_positions`):** `_identify_candidates` scans ONLY the named positions and **bypasses the CamSol/ESM pre-filter** within scope (raises the candidate cap to cover them all); empty scope в†’ `[]` (caller errors, no full-chain fallback). `_recommendation`/`_generate_summary`/the router one-liner handle `ddg=None`. Tiering POLICY (scope parse, tier triggers, estimate) lives in `tool_router`; `scan()`'s own default stays `run_rosetta=True` for backward-compatible direct callers. **Coverage + lossless data model (2026-06-09):** `scan()` gains `rosetta_shortlist_k` (None = FULL grid default вЂ” Rosetta on every candidate; int = SHORTLIST top-K by fast score, the rest RETAINED as `not_computed`, never dropped) and `ddg_basis` ("symmetric" default / "asymmetric"). The candidate-generation 20-cap is REMOVED (default `max_candidates=None`) в†’ the full positionsГ—`candidates_per_pos` grid is generated and CamSol/ESM-scored (lossless; in-chat display still summarises top-N). **Every result record is now keyed by `key`=(from,pos,to) and carries `ddg_basis`, `tier` ("fast"/"deep"), `fast_score`, and the existing per-measure fields** вЂ” substrate for the future Excel export + cross-layer aggregate scoring; deferred candidates get explicit `not_computed` markers, never 0.0/blank. **ThermoMPNN fast-tier voter (2026-06-09):** `scan(run_thermompnn=True)` calls `_run_thermompnn` in the fast pass в†’ per-candidate `thermompnn_ddg`/`thermompnn_source` added to each record (chain-aware key). `present_voters_score(rosetta_ddg, thermompnn_ddg, camsol, esm, вЂ¦)` renormalises over the voters PRESENT вЂ” both ddG voters absent в†’ exactly 0.6В·camsol+0.4В·esm (graceful == pre-ThermoMPNN, byte-for-byte). Keep-both (C): Rosetta + ThermoMPNN are independent voters (learned GNN vs physics relax) вЂ” both retained when present so their agreement feeds the future aggregate-confidence layer. **Residue-identity fix (2026-06-09):** the candidate identity is now the **author resnum (+chain)**, not the sequence index. `scan()` builds the coordinate-ordered residue spine (`ordered_chain_residues`), uses the coordinate sequence for CamSol/ESM (so seqindexв†”resnum is exact), and each record carries `resnum`/`icode` (identity в†’ Rosetta/ThermoMPNN/scope/viz/display, via the `position` field) + `seqindex` (derived в†’ CamSol/ESM). **Fixes a pre-existing SHIPPED bug** where `candidate["position"]` (1-based seqindex) was treated as the author resnum by scope, the candidate key, viz, AND the gold-tier Rosetta path (`pdb2pose`) вЂ” silently wrong on any non-1-start/gapped chain; masked because all prior structures were 1-based-contiguous. Scope ("residues 30-45" = AUTHOR 30-45), Rosetta (`_run_rosetta_batch` passes resnum), and viz now address by author resnum. Legacy fallback (no PDB) keeps resnum==seqindex. **RaSP physics-proxy voter + AXIS-AWARE handoff (2026-06-10):** `scan(run_rasp=True)` calls `_run_rasp` в†’ per-candidate `rasp_ddg`/`rasp_source`. `present_voters_score` is now AXIS-AWARE: PHYSICS is ONE slot = **Rosetta if computed for that candidate, ELSE RaSP** (the proxy) вЂ” Rosetta and RaSP NEVER both vote (RaSP is a Rosetta surrogate, so it HANDS OFF per candidate, no additive double-count). When Rosetta is present, RaSP's score contribution в†’ 0 but its value is RETAINED and the **`rasp_minus_rosetta` proxy-QC delta** is stored; records also carry `physics_source` (rosetta\|rasp\|not_computed). ThermoMPNN (ML/static axis), CamSol (solubility), ESM (fitness) unchanged. `RASP_WEIGHT`/`w_rasp` are PROVISIONAL вЂ” the В§9 aggregate-weighting benchmark (independence Г— confidence) calibrates the physics-axis weight later (proxy < real); the handoff MECHANISM is what's built now. Live-verified: non-1-start chain в†’ RaSP 12/12 mapped, cross-source identity holds; deep candidate в†’ physics=Rosetta, RaSP retained + delta stored; RaSP-disabled scan == pre-RaSP byte-for-byte. **DynaMut2 DYNAMICS-axis voter (2026-06-10):** `scan(run_dynamut2=True)` calls `_run_dynamut2` on the DEEP candidate set (rides the deep opt-in; remote API в†’ SPARSE, capped by `DYNAMUT2_MAX_CANDIDATES`, top-N by fast score, rest dynamics not_computed), CONCURRENT with Rosetta (a thread вЂ” wall в‰€ max(rosetta, dynamut2), remote I/O vs local CPU). `present_voters_score` gains a DYNAMICS slot that is **INDEPENDENT вЂ” always counted when present, NEVER zeroed/handed off (the inverse of the RaSP handoff)**; records carry `dynamut2_ddg`/`dynamut2_source`. SIGN-NORMALISED via the SHARED `rosetta_bridge.normalize_dynamut2_ddg` (DynaMut2 reports positive=STABILISING вЂ” OPPOSITE; `DYNAMUT2_DDG_SIGN`=в€’1). **Empirical fallbacks are EXCLUDED** from the dynamics axis (a BLOSUM/B-factor estimate is not dynamics в†’ not_computed). Reuses the author-resnum identity + chain-aware key (round-trips cleanly; no SSM alignment needed). GRACEFUL: API failure/disabled/over-cap в†’ dynamics not_computed; the deep run (Rosetta + others) is UNAFFECTED. Live-verified: all 4 axes present on one residue (1-start + non-1-start), sign correct on buried L99 (+1.9 destabilising), API failure в†’ deep completes. |

| `sequence_viewer.py` | `build_scf_file()`, `build_scf_runscript()`, `ensure_sequence_viewer_commands()`, `dock_sequences_bottom_command()`, `build_numbering_header_content()`, `numbering_header_command()`, `left_click_select_command()`, `lean_layout_commands()`, `default_presentation_commands()`, `apply_lean_layout()`, `apply_default_presentation()`, `consolidated_viewers_command()`, `disentangle_chain_command()`, `resolve_group_edit_target()` | вњ… Complete (foundation + CamSol + consolidation) | **Sequence-Viewer integration layer + deterministic layout/presentation.** `lean_layout_commands()`/`default_presentation_commands()` return the `config.CHIMERAX_*` lists (config-driven, NOT LLM, NOT `preset`); `apply_lean_layout(run_command)`/`apply_default_presentation(run_command)` run them **error-first** (a failing command is recorded and the rest continue вЂ” an open is never aborted). Layout = once per session (guarded in the bridge); presentation = per open. **Sequence-Viewer integration layer.** PART A (bidirectional click highlighting): `ensure_sequence_viewer_commands(model_id, chains)` в†’ `sequence chain #M/CH` opens + auto-associates the chain (selecting in 3D highlights the column; dragging the sequence selects in 3D вЂ” native once associated). The `open` path already auto-shows the sequence (`chimerax_bridge._maybe_show_sequence_on_open`, `CHIMERAX_SHOW_SEQUENCE_ON_OPEN`) вЂ” **per chain** for multimers and **re-docked to the bottom, stacked**: `dock_sequences_bottom_command()` writes a `runscript` loader that drives the Qt dock widget (`main_window.addDockWidget(BottomDockWidgetArea)` + `splitDockWidget(вЂ¦, Vertical)`) because ChimeraX 1.11.1 has no REST command to set a tool's dock area (verified live). **PART C (residue-number ruler):** each per-chain viewer gets a numbering ruler labelled every N residues with the **ACTUAL PDB resnums** (auth seq IDs). 1.11.1's native numbering is POSITION-based (`seq_canvas._compute_numbering = numbering_start + count`, a linear offset reading 1..N that can't honor gaps вЂ” probed live), so `build_numbering_header_content(ordered_resnums, interval)` builds a ruler string placing each label's units digit at its column via `chain_resnum_to_seqpos` (consistent with the MPNN alignment numbering; non-1-start в†’ 2,12,22 not 1,11,21; gap-aware) and `numbering_header_command(model,chain,resnums,interval)` adds it as a custom `alignment.add_fixed_header("Numbering", вЂ¦)` via a `runscript` (no `sequence` numbering command exists). `chimerax_bridge._model_chain_resnums` supplies each chain's resnums (`info residues` scoped to `~solvent & ~ligand & ~ions`, sorted); run error-first per chain (a failure never disrupts the open). `left_click_select_command(enable)` toggles `mousemode left select` (PyMOL-style; off by default). PART B (SCF colouring mirror): `open *.scf` is **unsupported over REST in 1.11.1** ("Unrecognized file suffix") в†’ `build_scf_file(residue_colors, ordered_resnums, out)` writes the `.scf` (resnumв†’0-based alignment col via `proteinmpnn_bridge.chain_resnum_to_seqpos`в€’1, RGB clamped) and `build_scf_runscript(scf, py)` writes a loader `.py` that drives `SequenceViewer.new_region(blocks=, fill=)`; REST command is `runscript "<py>"`. Scratch under `config.SEQVIEW_CACHE_DIR` (`.as_posix()`). Error-first (consumers degrade, never break structure colouring). **CamSol is wired** (`CamsolBridge._build_sequence_viewer_viz`); other consumers are a В§9 fast-follow. **PART D (sequence-viewer CONSOLIDATION):** `consolidated_viewers_command(threshold,cap,interval,numbering)` вЂ” when chain count > threshold (default 3) and в‰¤ cap (default 8), opens ONE alignment window per unique sequence group instead of N per-chain panels. **GROUPING KEY = (seq_hash[:12], resnums_tuple)** вЂ” stable across sessions, handles different numbering. One ROW per structure Г— group; `session.alignments.new_alignment(reps, identify_as="grp_"+hash)` auto-associates ALL chains with matching sequences in ALL open models (clicking the О± row selects all О± copies вЂ” native ChimeraX). Group ident is deterministic (`grp_HASH`) so `new_alignment` auto-destroys prior alignments with the same ident (idempotent reconsolidate). Each group alignment gets its own Numbering ruler (same algorithm as per-chain). **Threshold/toggle** (config-exposed via `CHIMERAX_SEQUENCE_CONSOLIDATE_THRESHOLD`): 1вЂ“3 chains в†’ per-chain unchanged; 4вЂ“8 в†’ consolidated; >8 в†’ whole-model fallback. **Disentangle:** `disentangle_chain_command(model_id, chain)` в†’ `sequence chain #M/C` opens a standalone viewer for one chain (breaking it out of its group). **Dynamic regroup:** `bridge.reconsolidate()` re-runs `consolidated_viewers_command` to rebuild groups after a sequence edit. **Edit disambiguation:** `resolve_group_edit_target(group_chains, requested_chain)` returns (chains, None) or (None, msg) вЂ” never silently edits the wrong target. Error-first per section (consolidated/per-chain/dock); a consolidation failure never disrupts the dock hook. **ADDRESSABILITY INVARIANT:** display-only; `#N/A` targeting completely unaffected. **Live-verified (2026-06-06):** 2HHB + 1BBB (8 chains = 4О± + 4ОІ) в†’ 2 group windows (`grp_af828e69a5f2` О±-group rows 2HHB:A,C + 1BBB:A,C; `grp_9287755aa6aa` ОІ-group) with Numbering rulers, instead of 8 separate panels. Reconsolidate idempotent (destroys old, recreates). Disentangle confirmed. See В§7 |
| `colabfold_bridge.py` | `ColabFoldBridge`, `predict()`, `estimate_runtime_s()`, `_build_worker()`, `is_available()` | вњ… Complete (v1) | AF2-quality sequenceв†’structure via the WSL2 `~/colabfold_env` (run via `wsl_bridge.COLABFOLD_PYTHON`). f-string worker (zero project imports, JSON in `/tmp`, copy back), **remote MSA server** (no local DBs). copiesв†’colon-joined homo-oligomer (multimer); optional custom template; num_models/num_recycle/`quick` preset. **Total-residue guard** `COLABFOLD_MAX_TOTAL_RESIDUES` (pre-launch + runtime CUDA-OOM catch в†’ clear message, never a raw traceback). Returns ranked PDB + per-residue/mean pLDDT + PAE + pTM(/ipTM) + PNG paths; input-hash cache `cache/colabfold_{hash}/`. NEVER raises (error-first dict). **JAX persistent compilation cache** (`COLABFOLD_JAX_COMPILE_CACHE_DIR`, WSL2 ext4) set on the `colabfold_batch` process so XLA reuses compiled executables across the fresh-per-fold workers вЂ” a different sequence skips most of the ~10-min recompile (measured 36-aa: cold 538s в†’ warm 287s, ~47%; partial because MSA-depth differs, see В§8). The bridge takes an explicit sequence; **the MPNN top-design auto-pull is wired at the ROUTER** (`tool_router._mpnn_top_sequence`, В§13 2026-06-06). DEFERRED: batch top-N, amber relax, single_sequence (see В§9) |
| `rfdiffusion_bridge.py` | `RFdiffusionBridge`, `is_available()`, `analyze()`, `run_handoff()`, `_dispatch()`; module fns `build_binder_contig`/`build_motif_contig`/`normalize_symmetry`/`_chain_extent` | рџџЎ Scaffold (not activated) | Real wrapper around the **verified v1 `run_inference.py` CLI**, gated behind `is_available()` (**False here** вЂ” no `~/rfdiffusion_env`; the live path never runs). **Single execution path:** `run_inference.py` ALWAYS dispatched via `wsl.exe` в†’ `wsl_bridge.RFDIFFUSION_PYTHON` (no native-Windows/Py-3.12 interpreter; **VENV312 removed from the RFdiffusion path entirely**). Availability records only the clone location (`win_clone` fs-check vs `wsl_clone` probe via `WSLBridge.check_rfdiffusion`) for `/mnt/c` path translation. **NLв†’contig/hotspot/symmetry parser** (binder target-range`/0` + binder-length + `ppi.hotspot_res`; motif keep-contig; symmetric `--config-name symmetry` + canonical `c4`/`d2`/named) reusing the proteinmpnn/selection resnum spine. **Content-hash cache** (`cache/rfdiffusion/`); **error-first** (never fabricates a backbone or claims a run). **`run_handoff`:** backbone в†’ EXISTING `ProteinMPNNBridge.analyze` в†’ `ColabFoldBridge.predict`. Activation (Py 3.9-3.11 WSL2 torch-cu128/dgl/SE3 on `sm_120` + weights) **deferred** вЂ” see `docs/rfdiffusion_activation_plan.md` |
| `log_analyser.py` | `display_stats()` | вњ… Complete | Parses JSONL session logs; `stats` command in REPL |
| `diag.py` | вЂ” | вњ… Complete | One-off diagnostic script; tests WSL2 availability + PyRosetta import |

## 4. Configuration Reference

### ChimeraX

| Constant | Default / Current value | Description |
|----------|------------------------|-------------|
| `CHIMERAX_PATH` | `C:\Users\andre\documents\ChimeraX 1.11.1\bin\ChimeraX.exe` | Path to ChimeraX executable |
| `REST_HOST` | `"127.0.0.1"` | REST server host |
| `REST_PORT` | `60001` | REST server port |
| `REST_TIMEOUT` | `10` | Seconds per HTTP request to ChimeraX |
| `CHIMERAX_SHOW_SEQUENCE_ON_OPEN` | `True` (env `вЂ¦=false` to disable) | After a successful structure open, open + associate the Sequence Viewer for the new model |
| `CHIMERAX_SEQUENCE_PER_CHAIN` / `вЂ¦_MAX` | `True` / `8` | Open one Sequence Viewer **per chain** (selectable separately, not collapsed to "chains A,B"); a structure with more chains than `вЂ¦_MAX` falls back to the single grouped viewer |
| `CHIMERAX_SEQUENCE_DOCK_BOTTOM` | `True` (env `вЂ¦=false` to disable) | Re-dock the Sequence Viewer(s) along the **bottom** edge, stacked vertically (via the Qt dock widget вЂ” no REST command exists) |
| `CHIMERAX_SEQUENCE_NUMBERING` / `вЂ¦_NUMBER_INTERVAL` | `True` / `10` | Add a residue-number **ruler** to each per-chain viewer (or consolidated group viewer), labelled every N residues with the **actual PDB resnums** (via `chain_resnum_to_seqpos`, consistent with MPNN numbering). Custom fixed header вЂ” 1.11.1's native numbering is position-based |
| `CHIMERAX_SEQUENCE_CONSOLIDATE_THRESHOLD` | `3` (env `CHIMERAX_SEQUENCE_CONSOLIDATE_THRESHOLD=N`) | Chain count above which per-chain viewers are consolidated into ONE alignment window per unique sequence group (fixes the "N chains letterbox the 3D view" problem). 1вЂ“3 chains в†’ per-chain unchanged; 4вЂ“8 в†’ consolidated; >8 в†’ whole-model fallback. A group = all chains with the same sequence string AND residue numbering map |
| `CHIMERAX_LEAN_LAYOUT` | `True` (env `вЂ¦=false`) | Apply the lean window layout once per session (hide Log / Command Line Interface / Toolbar; menubar + title bar kept) |
| `CHIMERAX_LEAN_LAYOUT_COMMANDS` | `["tool hide Log", 'tool hide "Command Line Interface"', "tool hide Toolbar"]` | The lean-layout command list (config-driven, NOT LLM, NOT `preset`); all verified live in 1.11.1 |
| `CHIMERAX_DEFAULT_PRESENTATION` | `True` (env `вЂ¦=false`) | Apply the deterministic default presentation per structure open (after load, before analysis colouring) |
| `CHIMERAX_DEFAULT_PRESENTATION_COMMANDS` | `["hide solvent atoms", "cartoon", "show ligand atoms", "style ligand stick", "color bychain", "color ligand byhetero", "set bgColor black", "lighting soft", "graphics silhouettes true", "view"]` | The presentation command list; all verified live in 1.11.1. Analysis colourings (CamSol/ESM/MPNN) run later and override the by-chain baseline; SCF sequence regions still land |
| `SEQVIEW_CACHE_DIR` | `cache/seqview/` | Scratch dir for `.scf` coloring files + their `runscript` loaders (forward-slash paths) |

### Anthropic / LLM

| Constant | Default / Current value | Description |
|----------|------------------------|-------------|
| `ANTHROPIC_MODEL` | `"claude-sonnet-4-6"` | Model used for translation |
| `TRANSLATOR_BACKEND` | `"claude"` | NLв†’ChimeraX translation backend: `"claude"` (Anthropic API, **default & active**) or `"ollama"` (local). Unknown в†’ claude |
| `TRANSLATOR_FALLBACK` | `True` | When active=claude, fall back to Ollama on a REAL Claude API failure (connection/timeout/auth/rate-limit). A successful-but-imperfect/refused response is NOT a trigger. Forced `"ollama"` NEVER falls back to Claude (benchmark honesty) |
| `OLLAMA_BASE_URL` | `"http://localhost:11434"` | Ollama server base URL |
| `OLLAMA_MODEL` | `"qwen3:8b"` | Exact model+tag (pulled + verified for schema-constrained structured output; fits the 12 GB RTX 5070 Ti) |
| `OLLAMA_NUM_CTX` | `16384` | Context window. StructureBot's system prompt (role + rules + full ChimeraX command reference) is **~7.5k tokens**, plus the targeted few-shot вЂ” so num_ctx must be в‰Ґ~10k or Ollama **silently truncates the prompt** (model never sees the rules/few-shot в†’ routing collapses; this was the dominant cause of the D1 engineering-tool failures). 16384 fits prompt+few-shot+generation and the 8B KV cache still fits the 12 GB card. **вљ  Over-sizing BEYOND VRAM** spills to CPU вЂ” slow + degrades constrained decoding; tune to your GPU |
| `TRANSLATOR_TOOL_NAMES` | 24 router literals | Canonical lowercase tool names the router dispatches on вЂ” ENUM-constrains the Ollama backend's `tools_needed` (constrained decoding cannot emit a misspelled/hallucinated/wrong-cased tool). A test asserts it вЉ‡ the `_dispatch_tool` registry |
| `OLLAMA_KEEP_ALIVE` | `"30s"` | Idle keep-alive before Ollama unloads from VRAM. SHORT; the explicit `ensure_translator_unloaded()` is the real contract (don't rely on the timer) |
| `OLLAMA_TIMEOUT` | `180` | Per-request HTTP timeout (a cold first-call model load can be slow) |
| `MAX_CONVERSATION_HISTORY` | `6` | Rolling history pairs (turns) |
| `AUTO_PROCEED_DELAY` | `2` | Seconds before auto-executing (0 = always prompt) |

### Stability / ddG

| Constant | Default | `.env.local` override | Description |
|----------|---------|----------------------|-------------|
| `ROSETTA_BACKEND` | `"auto"` | **`"local"`** в†ђ ACTIVE | Backend: `auto`/`dynamut2`/`empirical`/`pyrosetta`/`local` |
| `ROSETTA_LOCAL_PATH` | `""` | вЂ” | Path to Rosetta binary dir (unused; local backend uses PyRosetta via WSL2) |
| `PYROSETTA_AVAILABLE` | `False` | вЂ” | Legacy flag for direct PyRosetta import (not the WSL2 path) |
| `ROSETTA_RELAX_CACHE` | `<project>/cache/rosetta_relaxed/` | вЂ” | Cached FastRelax'd PDB files (keyed by MD5) |
| `ROSETTA_STRIP_WATERS` | `True` (strip) | `false` to preserve | Strip crystallographic HOH before PyRosetta (default; validated, standard practice). Set `False` to opt into **preserve** (re-append HOH; validated only on buried-water T26A). Preserve-all-static is a Rosetta anti-pattern вЂ” proper fix = selective buried-only/movable (Build Queue В§9). Relax cache is namespaced by mode (`_wat` suffix for preserve) |
| `relax_cycles` (param, not env) | `3` | вЂ” | `_run_rosetta_local()` parameter: FastRelax cycles for the per-mutation mutant relax + symmetric WT re-relax. Default 3 = production protocol (unchanged); exposed only so the convergence diagnostic can sweep 3/5/8. Cached WT baseline relax unaffected |
| `ROSETTA_MAX_WORKERS` | `8` | e.g. `12` | Deep-tier (Rosetta) pool size вЂ” independent per-mutation FastRelax units run via `multiprocessing.Pool` inside the one WSL2 worker (FIX D). Default 8 = i9-14900HX **P-core** count; do NOT set to the 32 logical threads (E-cores ВЅ-speed, HT, single-channel DDR5, 140 W throttle). Runtime-capped by `resolve_rosetta_workers` в†’ `min(this, ROSETTA_PHYSICAL_CORESв€’2, ROSETTA_WSL_MEM_BUDGET_MB/ROSETTA_WORKER_FOOTPRINT_MB)` |
| `ROSETTA_PHYSICAL_CORES` | `os.cpu_count()` | **`24`** on this box | Physical cores for the CPU cap (leaves 2 headroom). Default is best-effort logical count; set to the true physical count (i9-14900HX = 24) |
| `ROSETTA_WSL_MEM_BUDGET_MB` | `12000` | вЂ” | WSL2 RAM the pool may use (default WSL = ~50% host = ~16 GB on 32 GB; 12 GB leaves host/Chrome headroom). Caps workers at budget Г· footprint |
| `ROSETTA_WORKER_FOOTPRINT_MB` | `1200` | вЂ” | Measured per-worker PyRosetta footprint (~1 GB on the 2HHB tetramer) + margin; the divisor for the memory cap |
| `ROSETTA_BASE_SEED` | `1` | вЂ” | Fixed base seed for `mutation_seed(base, key, traj)` в†’ deterministic, reproducible ddG AND the parallel==serial identical-results contract (ranking/sign are seed-independent regardless) |
| `ROSETTA_PER_MUT_BASE_SEC` / `_BASE_RES` / `_EXPONENT` | `10` / `46` / `1.8` | вЂ” | **Deep-tier runtime-estimate calibration (estimate-honesty fix, 2026-06-09).** `per_mutation_sec(n) = BASE_SEC Г— (n/BASE_RES)^EXP` вЂ” SUPER-linear in pose size, anchored to measured points (1CRN 46 res в‰€ 10 s/mutation; 2HHB 574 res в‰і 733 s, killed-before-finish lower bound в†’ model gives ~940 s, biased high). Replaces the old flat ~25 s/position constant that ignored pose size |
| `ROSETTA_SHORTLIST_K` | `15` | вЂ” | Deep-tier **shortlist** size вЂ” when the user opts into "shortlist", Rosetta validates the fast tier's top-K by combined score; the rest are RETAINED as `not_computed` (never dropped). FULL grid is the default; shortlist is offered (with its own estimate) when the full-grid estimate exceeds `ROSETTA_FULL_GRID_OFFER_SEC` |
| `ROSETTA_FULL_GRID_OFFER_SEC` | `300` | вЂ” | When the full-grid deep estimate exceeds this, the confirm/tier surface presents BOTH full and shortlist options with distinct estimates (data-vs-speed is an explicit choice, never silent) |
| `ROSETTA_DDG_BASIS` | `"symmetric"` | `asymmetric` | ddG basis. **symmetric** (default) = per-mutation paired WT re-relax (variance-reduced). **asymmetric** (opt-in via "asymmetric") = score each mutant against the single cached global-WT relax вЂ” ~2Г— faster, noisier, **labelled in output**; the two are never mixed in one scan |
| `ROSETTA_PARALLEL_EFF_REF_RES` | `574` | вЂ” | Estimate large-pose guard (BUILD 3): at/below this (the 2HHB anchor) the `/workers` divisor is trusted; ABOVE it, parallel efficiency = REF/n_res (<1) shrinks the effective worker count so the estimate stays BIASED HIGH for bandwidth-bound big complexes (never undershoots) |
| `ROSETTA_WORKER_BASE_MB` / `_MB_PER_RES` | `500` / `2.2` | вЂ” | **Pose-size-scaled per-worker footprint (FIX 2).** `worker_footprint_mb(n) = BASE + PER_RESГ—n` вЂ” calibrated to 2HHB (8 workers в‰€ 1.75 GB each @ 574 res в†’ ~1763 MB в‡’ cap_mem 6, not the lucky 8). `resolve_rosetta_workers` uses this so the pool shrinks for large complexes and never oversubscribes WSL into swap. `ROSETTA_WORKER_FOOTPRINT_MB` (flat 1200) is now only the fallback when pose size is unknown |

Kept = the Rosetta deep weight for now; the В§9 aggregate-weighting benchmark lowers the proxy (proxy < real). RaSP NEVER votes alongside Rosetta вЂ” it hands off |
| `RASP_VERSION_TAG` | `rasp-v1;sign=1;ds10;port=вЂ¦` | Folded into the result cache key alongside (pdb-hash, chain) so a sign/model/port change BUSTS the cache instead of serving stale ddG |
| `RASP_TIMEOUT` / `RASP_CACHE_DIR` | `600` / `cache/rasp` | Worker wall-clock budget; per-(pdb,chain,version) ddG cache. **CPU ~tens of s/chain** (CNN ds-ensemble is the cost, not preprocessing ~1 s); cache makes a re-scan free. No GPU needed (small CNN; preprocessing is CPU regardless). **KNOWN LIMITATION вЂ” insertion codes:** RaSP's clean step (pdbfixer) STRIPS insertion codes, so an insertion-coded chain yields fewer residues than the original в†’ the WT-anchored alignment length-diverges в†’ **the WHOLE chain is not_computed** for RaSP (safe вЂ” never mis-attributes; ThermoMPNN + Rosetta still cover it). This means **antibody / Kabat- or IMGT-numbered structures (Fabs, scFvs) get NO RaSP physics-proxy** вЂ” relevant for CHO/HEK biologics work. Future refinement: an icode-preserving clean step (or re-anchor RaSP's renumbered output through a 1:1 pre-cleanв†”post-clean residue map) |
| `DYNAMUT2_DDG_SIGN` | `-1` | **The DynaMut2 sign вЂ” defined ONCE** (`rosetta_bridge.normalize_dynamut2_ddg`, used by BOTH the single-mutation parser and the double-mutant mm path). DynaMut2 reports positive=STABILISING (mCSM family) вЂ” OPPOSITE the system. EMPIRICALLY VERIFIED on 2LZM: L99A (exp +5.0 destabilising) в†’ DynaMut2 raw в€’3.32 в†’ system +3.32. вљ  The pre-2026-06-10 code used the raw value (NO flip) в†’ it shipped INVERTED DynaMut2 ddG (see В§13) |
| `DYNAMUT2_MM_SIGN_VERIFIED` | `false` | The SINGLE-mutation sign is EMPIRICALLY VERIFIED (live battery: correlation +0.75/+0.81 vs exp, L99A destabiliser +3.32, A149V stabiliser в€’0.38). The MULTIPLE-mutation (prediction_mm) sign is only INFERRED (endpoint chronically ERRORs). **ENFORCED GUARD (not just a flag):** while False, a returned mm result is treated as **NOT_COMPUTED** вЂ” the sign-normalised mm value is NEVER emitted; the pair falls to the additive fallback (a sum of the VERIFIED single-mutant ddGs) with a surfaced warning. So even if the endpoint recovers, the inferred mm sign cannot leak into output. Set True ONLY after a live mm anti-symmetry/known-mutation check. The mm fixture sign-corrections are as provisional as this |
| `DYNAMUT2_ENABLE` | `"auto"` | DYNAMICS-axis voter toggle. `"auto"` = use when WSL/API reachable; `"false"` disables (deep run == pre-DynaMut2). Tests gate it OFF (conftest) so no test hits the remote API implicitly |
| `DYNAMUT2_MAX_CANDIDATES` | `25` | Cap per deep run (remote API в†’ can't do hundreds). Over cap в†’ cover top-N by fast score; the rest dynamics not_computed (never silently dropped) |
| `DYNAMUT2_WEIGHT` | `0.45` | **PROVISIONAL вЂ” pending benchmark.** DYNAMICS-axis weight; INDEPENDENT (always counted when present, no handoff). Calibration note: DynaMut2 shares experimental supervision with ThermoMPNN в†’ partial correlation, to be handled in the В§9 benchmark. Concurrency: DynaMut2 (remote I/O) overlaps Rosetta (local CPU) so deep wall в‰€ max, not sum. `DYNAMUT2_MAX_WORKERS`=4 (existing) governs intra-batch concurrency |

### Double Mutant Scoring

| Constant | Default | Description |
|----------|---------|-------------|
| `DOUBLE_MUTANT_DISTANCE_THRESHOLD_FAR` | `10.0` | CО±-CО± distance (Г…) above which DynaMut2 is reliable for double mutants |
| `DOUBLE_MUTANT_DISTANCE_THRESHOLD_CLOSE` | `4.0` | CО±-CО± distance (Г…) below which PyRosetta is required (close pairs) |
| `DOUBLE_MUTANT_MAX_PAIRS` | `500` | Max pairs to consider before distance-based routing |
| `DOUBLE_MUTANT_TOP_N` | `10` | Default number of top-ranked pairs to return |
| `DOUBLE_MUTANT_DESTABILISING_DDG` | `2.0` | О”О”G (kcal/mol) above which a mutation is "clearly destabilising". Stability mode drops a pair only when **both** mutations exceed this; `ddg=0.0` (DynaMut2 neutral/unknown) is never filtered |
| `DOUBLE_MUTANT_ADDITIVE_FALLBACK` | `True` | When True, pairs with no epistasis-aware backend available (DynaMut2 mm API down, or close pair with PyRosetta disabled) are scored additively (ddG_A + ddG_B, epistasis=0) instead of dropped |

## 5. Critical Conventions

### Subprocess rules (wsl_bridge.py, enforced everywhere)
All subprocess calls that interact with Windows console handles **must** use:
```python
stdin=subprocess.DEVNULL
creationflags=subprocess.CREATE_NO_WINDOW
```
Rationale: `wsl.exe` calls `SetConsoleMode()` on the inherited stdin handle, which permanently disables `ReadConsole()` for the rest of the process lifetime, breaking the Rich REPL.

### Path handling rule
All file paths passed to ChimeraX commands **must** use `.as_posix()` to produce forward slashes. ChimeraX on Windows rejects backslashes in `save "..."` and `open "..."` commands.
```python
cx_fwd = Path(some_path).as_posix()
result = bridge.run_command(f'save "{cx_fwd}"')
```

### Worker script rules (ESM worker, ESMFold worker, PyRosetta worker, double mutant PyRosetta worker)
Worker scripts that run in subprocesses or WSL2 **must**:
1. Have zero imports from the StructureBot project
2. Communicate exclusively via JSON files (never stdin/stdout for structured data)
3. Write a result file even on exception (`try/except` at the outermost level)
4. Use `flush=True` on all print calls
5. PyRosetta workers: use double-braces `{{...}}` throughout (embedded in Python f-string)

### ChimeraX selector ordering rule
In ChimeraX commands, specifiers must appear in this order to avoid syntax errors:
```
#{model}/{chain}:{residue}@{atom}
```
Example: `#1/A:82@CA` вЂ” model first, then chain, then residue, then atom.

### Primary model guard
Commands that should only act on the first loaded model must use `#1` explicitly. The translator's static system prompt instructs Claude to always emit `#1` for single-model operations.

### f-string double-brace rule in worker scripts
The PyRosetta and double-mutant worker scripts are embedded as Python f-strings. Any literal `{...}` that should appear in the worker code must be written as `{{...}}`. Only actual f-string interpolations from the outer scope use single braces (e.g., `{wsl_pdb!r}`, `{mut_list_json!r}`).

### Error-first return convention (all bridges)
All bridge `analyze()` methods return `ToolStepResult` вЂ” they **never raise**. On failure, `result.success = False` and `result.error` contains the message. Callers check `result.success` and degrade gracefully.

### Windows UTF-8 stdout convention (canonical fix 2026-06-07)
`tests/conftest.py` and `main.py` both call `sys.stdout.reconfigure(encoding="utf-8")` / `sys.stderr.reconfigure(encoding="utf-8")` guarded by `if sys.platform == "win32" and hasattr(sys.stdout, "reconfigure")`. This is the **canonical fix** вЂ” after reconfigure, all Python print() calls can freely use О±, ОІ, в†’, в‰Ґ and any Unicode character. **Do NOT degrade scientific Unicode (О±, ОІ, etc.) to ASCII.** Arrow `в†’` in display/debug strings may use `->` for brevity; Greek letters stay Unicode everywhere (data, files, console).

`console.print()` from Rich is always safe and exempt. The `_safe_print`/`_pprint` ASCII-fallback wrappers in `rosetta_bridge.py`/`disulfide_bridge.py` predate the reconfigure fix and remain as defensive fallbacks; new code should rely on the reconfigure instead.

### Double mutant mode detection (in `_run_double_mutant`)
Epitope keywords: `"epitope"`, `"binding"`, `"interface"`, `"preserve"`, `"target"` в†’ `mode = "epitope"`. Otherwise в†’ `mode = "stability"`. PyRosetta keywords: `"pyrosetta"`, `"rosetta"`, `"accurate"`, `"high accuracy"`, `"validate"` в†’ `run_pyrosetta = True`.

### Double mutant ddG / fallback semantics
- **`ddg=0.0` is neutral/unknown, not destabilising.** The stability-mode pair filter excludes a pair only when **both** mutations have `ddg > DOUBLE_MUTANT_DESTABILISING_DDG` (default +2.0 kcal/mol). A single `ddg=0.0` mutation never eliminates a pair. (Earlier logic required at least one *beneficial* mutation, which collapsed the candidate set to ~2 pairs whenever DynaMut2 returned all-zero О”О”G.)
- **Additive fallback never drops a pair.** When no epistasis-aware backend is available вЂ” DynaMut2 mm API down, circuit breaker tripped, or a close pair with `run_pyrosetta=False` вЂ” `_apply_additive_fallback()` scores the pair as `ddG_A + ddG_B` with `epistasis=0.0` and `backend_used="additive_fallback"`, and appends a warning. Set `DOUBLE_MUTANT_ADDITIVE_FALLBACK=False` to drop such pairs instead.

All WSL/ChimeraX calls mocked вЂ” no live fold in CI.

Run commands:
```bash
# Full suite (excludes slow benchmarks)
pytest tests/ --ignore=tests/test_rosetta_benchmark.py -q

# Including benchmark collection check
pytest tests/ -q --collect-only

# PyRosetta benchmarks (slow, requires WSL2+PyRosetta)
pytest tests/test_rosetta_benchmark.py -m benchmark -v --timeout=1800 -s

# Double mutant tests only
pytest tests/test_double_mutant_bridge.py -v

# Single benchmark spot-check
pytest tests/test_rosetta_benchmark.py -m benchmark -v -s -k "t4_l99a"
```

**Note:** `pytest.ini` now registers `benchmark`, `slow`, and `timeout` as known markers вЂ” no more `PytestUnknownMarkWarning`.

## 7. Validated Live Results

The following results have been confirmed working against **1HSG** (HIV-1 protease, PDB ID 1HSG, homodimer, chains A+B, ligand MK1):

| Feature | Validated result |
|---------|-----------------|
| CamSol solubility scan | Chain A scored; aggregation-prone residues coloured red in ChimeraX |
| ESM-2 conservation | Chain A scored; conserved residues blue, variable red |
| Mutation scan (full pipeline) | Top candidate `I64E` (О”О”G = в€’3.53 kcal/mol by DynaMut2); `V82A` reference used in tests |
| V82A ddG (DynaMut2) | ~+1.5 to +2.0 kcal/mol (Mahalingam et al.); used as benchmark reference |
| Assembly analysis | 1HSG detected as homodimer (A2 stoichiometry); interface residues between chains A+B stored |
| Disulfide candidates | Chain Aв†”B candidates with CОІ-CОІ < 4.5 Г… ranked by geometry+ESM+stability |
| Proline scan | П†-angle candidates on chain A; functional residue exclusion when active-site set |
| Glycan scan | NXS/T sequons on chain A scored for surface exposure, SS content, ESM tolerance |
| ProteinMPNN redesign | Chain A sequences generated; 3 top designs validated with ESMFold. **Designs now persist to `cache/proteinmpnn/` and are retrievable/alignable without re-running.** WT-vs-redesign alignment **live-verified in ChimeraX** (2026-06-01): a 79%-changed redesign of 1IL8 вЂ” WT row auto-associated to chains A+B "with 0 mismatches", the heavily-changed redesign row did not (as expected), so the ungapped 1:1 columns map to the right 3D residues through the WT association (`sequence associate` force-assoc also works). **Auto-decoration live-verified**: a known-change redesign в†’ the 3D selection equalled exactly the changed residues `[5,20,35,50,65]` and changed residue 5's `ribbon_color` = `255,99,71` (tomato) вЂ” sequence highlight, structure colour, and columnв†”3D mapping all consistent |
| Salt bridge analysis | Asp/Gluв†”Arg/Lys/His contacts within 4 Г… on chain A |
| Sequence-Viewer click highlighting (Part A) | **Live-verified (2026-06-02)**: opening 1HSG auto-opens + associates the Sequence Viewer (`n_associations=1`, `assoc_keys="chain A"`); with the chain associated, ChimeraX natively mirrors 3Dв†”sequence selection (`select #1/A:50` runs clean; Ctrl-click a 3D residue highlights its column and dragging a sequence span selects in 3D). Optional `mousemode left select` toggle for PyMOL-style click (off by default) |
| Sequence-Viewer colour mirror вЂ” CamSol (Part B) | **Live-verified (2026-06-02)**: a real CamSol scan of 1HSG chain A wrote a `.scf` + `runscript` that created **4 colour regions** in the Sequence Viewer (red/tomato/dodger-blue/blue) with **0 command errors**. Position alignment spot-check: hot-spot residue **50** в†’ SCF alignment column **49** в†’ region colour `(255,0,0)` red, matching the 3D command `color #1/A:50 red` exactly. `open *.scf` is unsupported over REST in 1.11.1 в†’ the `runscript`+`new_region` path is what works |
| Live selection as input | **Live-verified (2026-06-02)** on 1HSG. **3D Ctrl-click** path: selecting chain-A residues 10/25/50, then `what's selected` в†’ "3 residue(s) вЂ¦ chain A: 10,25,50", and `scan the selection` в†’ CamSol for exactly those (A:10 z=+0.60 soluble, A:25 z=+0.69 soluble, A:50 z=в€’2.08 aggregation-prone) with the residues coloured in 3D (A:50в†’red `255,0,0`, A:10в†’dodger-blue `30,144,255`). **Sequence-Viewer** path: a selection made through the alignment association (columnsв†’residues 60вЂ“64) appears identically in `info residues sel`, and `what is selected` / `scan the selection` report `60-64` and their per-residue scores вЂ” confirming both UIs feed the **same** capture path. Empty selection в†’ graceful message (not an error) |
| Lean layout + default presentation | **Live-verified (2026-06-02)** via the real bridge post-open hooks on 1HSG: Log / Command Line Interface / Toolbar all hidden (`tool[...].shown=False`), menubar + title bar kept; black background, silhouettes on; waters hidden (`HOH shown 0.0`), MK1 ligand shown as **stick** (`draw_mode=2`), chains distinct by colour (A vs B different ribbon RGB), Sequence Viewer open + associated to both chains; `view` framed. A subsequent CamSol scan **overrode the by-chain baseline** (chain A residue 50 ribbon в†’ `(255,0,0)` red, chain B still bychain) **and** the SCF sequence regions still landed. REST `color`/`select`/`runscript` confirmed working with the Command Line hidden |
| Ollama local translation backend | **Live-verified (2026-06-02)** вЂ” Ollama 0.24.0 + **`qwen3:8b`** (6.6 GB, 100% GPU on the RTX 5070 Ti), forced `TRANSLATOR_BACKEND=ollama`, schema-constrained JSON (`format`+`think:false`, temp 0). All outputs schema-valid (7 keys); simple prompts produce clean, runnable commands on 1HSG вЂ” "color chain A red"в†’`color #1/A red`, "hide chain B"в†’`hide #1/B`, "show chain A as cartoon"в†’`cartoon #1/A`, **0 ChimeraX errors** each (~7вЂ“11 s/translation). **Quality caveat (benchmark signal):** the local 8B is rougher than Claude on complex prompts (e.g. wrong tool-name casing, an occasional forbidden `preset publication` / malformed zone tail) вЂ” exactly why it's the benchmark+fallback role, not the default. The backend-agnostic `_sanitize_zone_syntax` guard fired on Ollama output unchanged; `_parse_response` hardened to drop stray non-string command elements (no-op for Claude) |
| Translator backend benchmark (Claude vs local) | **DEFINITIVE run 2026-06-03 on the cleaned serving config** (`scripts/translator_benchmark_results.md`, commit `0e08e5b`: num_ctx=16384, enum-constrained tools, case-insensitive routing, explicit sampling `seed=0`, targeted few-shot), Ollama **`qwen3:8b` Q4_K_M**, **93-case held-out EVAL_CORPUS Г— 11 categories (в‰Ґ8 each)**, **N = 5 runs (mean [minвЂ“max])**, forced backends (no fallback). **SCORES ROUTING + COMMAND SYNTAX ONLY вЂ” `tool_inputs` (arguments/scope) are NOT checked, so this is *not* an end-to-end correctness number** (the argument/scope upgrade is an open В§9 item). **Claude (reference): FULL 99% [99вЂ“99], RAW 99% [98вЂ“99], routing 99%, schema 99%, lat med 5.3 s** (the 5 "errors" are transient API failures over the run). **qwen3:8b: FULL 92% [92вЂ“92], RAW 88% [87вЂ“88], routing 93%, schema 100%, lat med 3.5 s, 0 errors.** **Per-category (Ollama FULL): camsol 89%, mpnn 78%, proline 75%, viz 88%, zone 89%; disulfide/esm/hide_show/multi_tool/rfdiffusion/selection_scope all 100%.** **The +35 pts over the prior 57% is ENTIRELY the serving-config fixes** вЂ” the failing engineering tools (camsol 0в†’89, selection 0в†’100, mpnn 18в†’78, esm 28в†’100) were a `num_ctx=8192` truncation throttle, NOT model weakness; **the prior 57% (commit `71e2779`) was measured on the throttled config and is discarded as not comparable.** **zone: RAW 42% [33вЂ“44] в†’ FULL 89%** вЂ” the deterministic guard still does the zone normalization (and the RAW range is the only cross-run variation; see determinism note). **Determinism:** Ollama runs 2вЂ“5 are byte-identical; run 1 (cold) differs only in zone RAW pre-guard syntax (cold-start GPU kernel choice), which the guard absorbs вЂ” so **FULL pass-rate is a stable 92% on all 5 runs**, byte-identical RAW holds warm-only. Audit trail: `SERVING_CONFIG_BILL_OF_HEALTH.md`. **Remaining gap to 100% is model routing/syntax** (camsol/mpnn/proline/viz/zone misses) вЂ” few-shot from the disjoint `EXAMPLE_POOL` or a stronger model, NOT the guards |
| Translator VRAM discipline + one-way fallback | **Live-verified (2026-06-02).** VRAM: after a forced-ollama translation `ollama ps` showed `qwen3:8b вЂ¦ 100% GPU` resident; `ensure_translator_unloaded()` (keep_alive=0) в†’ `ollama ps` **empty** (VRAM freed); it fires from `tool_router._dispatch_tool` before any GPU bridge and is a no-op under Claude. **Fallback claudeв†’ollama**: with `TRANSLATOR_BACKEND=claude` + fallback on and Claude pointed at an unreachable base URL в†’ `APIConnectionError` в†’ logged "falling back to the local Ollama backend" в†’ still translated "hide chain B"в†’`hide #1/B`. **Forced ollama down**: `TRANSLATOR_BACKEND=ollama` with the Ollama URL unreachable в†’ `ConnectionError` surfaced and **Claude was never called** (benchmark honesty) |
| Cavity detection | Internal voids in chain A ranked by burial depth and size |
| Double mutant bridge | **Validated end-to-end** (live): scan в†’ "suggest double mutant combinations" produces the 171в†’79 candidate funnel, routes/scoВ­res pairs, and prints the Rich Panel + ChimeraX viz. 42 unit tests pass; stability filter yields the full candidate set (~79 pairs vs the prior collapse to 2); close pairs scored additively when PyRosetta disabled |
| Validate-design fold-preservation (RMSD) axis | **Verified live against real ChimeraX 1.11.1** (2026-06-01). Parses BOTH RMSDs from `RMSD between N pruned atom pairs is X; (across all M pairs: Y)` в†’ **headline = all-pairs Y** (honest overall drift; pruned X flatters by dropping the worst residues), keeps pruned X + counts N/M. **Concentration** (free): gap = Yв€’X, pruned_fraction = (Mв€’N)/M в†’ descriptor (low/uniform В· concentrated В· broadly divergent). **Localized**: per-residue CО± deviation via an independent numpy **Kabsch** fit on the local design+reference PDBs (ChimeraX exposes no per-residue RMSD attribute over REST), в†’ top-K deviant residues + the design **coloured by deviation** (blueв†’red, reusing the CamSol grouped-`color` idiom) live during execute. Live check (1HSG chain A vs B): 99 matched, own-Kabsch all-pairs 0.4 (== matchmaker), deviations 0.07вЂ“1.06 Г… peaking at the flap loops (res 49/72/44/63/73); 18 colour commands landed, 0 errors. Locked by real-string + Kabsch unit tests |

**PyRosetta Benchmark Run 1 (2026-05-29)** вЂ” 11 mutations from ProThermDB:

| Metric | Result |
|--------|--------|
| Sign accuracy | 6/10 = 60% (I64E excluded, no precise experimental value) |
| Within 2.0 kcal/mol | 4/10 = 40% |
| MAE | 3.823 kcal/mol |
| RMSE | 5.492 kcal/mol |
| Pearson r | в€’0.059 (driven negative by A98V outlier: +14.52 predicted vs в€’0.5 experimental) |

Protocol suitable for sign prediction on surface-exposed mutations (4/6 correct for non-buried, non-interface positions); not reliable for buried mutations or magnitude accuracy. Without the A98V outlier, r в‰€ +0.46 and RMSE в‰€ 2.58 kcal/mol. Full analysis in `scripts/rosetta_validation_notes.md`.

### PyRosetta ddG protocol status (current, standalone validation 2026-05-29)

The local PyRosetta path is confirmed **working for ranking** but **not for calibrated absolute magnitudes**:

- **1HSG control panel** (`test_pyrosetta_ddg_controls.py`): buried-charge в‰« surface separation is correct (e.g. L90K +12.1, surface I72R в‰€ 0); sign behaviour sensible.
- **T4 lysozyme cross-check** (`test_pyrosetta_ddg_t4lysozyme.py`, 2LZM, 10 literature mutations): **sign accuracy 100%, Pearson r = +0.487** (vs Run 1's в€’0.059), but **MAE 3.92 / RMSE 5.23** вЂ” systematic **over-prediction**, worst on large cavities (L99A +12 vs exp +5; L133A +15 vs +2.7).
- **Aggregation diagnostic** (`test_pyrosetta_aggregation_diag.py`, 5 trajectories Г— 3 mutations): per-trajectory **spread в‰€ 8 kcal/mol** (two-sided noise). Aggregator MAE: **median 2.79 < mean 3.51 < min 3.84** в†’ **MEDIAN is the right aggregator**; MIN is refuted (drags noisy surface mutations to false stabilising values).
- **Convergence-vs-bias diagnostic** (`test_pyrosetta_convergence_diag.py`, completed 2026-05-29): swept relax_cycles 3/5/8 (median of 5 each). Verdict: **convergence-fixable (partial)**. More cycles move every median toward experiment and shrink spread (7.61в†’5.13 kcal/mol), but at 8+8 only ~half the gap closes вЂ” L99A +9.24в†’+7.30 (exp +5.0), V87M +7.24в†’+5.37 (exp +1.5; residual cavity-fill bias cycles don't clear), N116D в€’1.70в†’+0.64 (converges to ~0). Confirmed design: **median aggregation + more relax cycles for a validation tier** вЂ” magnitudes remain approximate, ranking reliable. Full notes in `scripts/rosetta_validation_notes.md`.

Bottom line: use PyRosetta ddG for **ranking + sign** (good), aggregate by **median**. The validation tier (median-of-N at higher cycle counts) roughly **halves** the magnitude error vs single-trajectory while leaving ranking unchanged вЂ” **see the confirmed 2LZM panel below**; absolute ddG is now tighter but should still be **disclosed as approximate (~В±2.7 kcal/mol RMSE)**.

### Validation-tier 2LZM panel вЂ” CONFIRMED (2026-05-30)

The required full re-run is done: the 10-mutation 2LZM panel scored at the validation tier (`validate_ddg`, **N=5 trajectories Г— 8+8 relax cycles, median**) via `scripts/validate_2lzm_panel.py`. Authoritative numbers in `scripts/validate_2lzm_results.json` (gitignored); full table + conclusion in `scripts/rosetta_validation_notes.md`.

| metric | validation tier (N=5 Г— 8+8) | 1-traj 2LZM | 1-traj Run 1 |
|--------|----------------------------:|------------:|-------------:|
| Sign accuracy | **90%** (9/10) | 100% | 60% |
| MAE (kcal/mol) | **2.586** | 3.92 | 3.823 |
| RMSE (kcal/mol) | **2.729** | 5.23 | 5.492 |
| Pearson r | **+0.499** | +0.487 | в€’0.059 |

**Thresholds (revised): r > 0.30 вњ… (+0.499) В· RMSE < 4.00 вњ… (2.729) В· sign в‰Ґ 60% вњ… (90%) вЂ” all PASS.** RMSE/MAE roughly halve vs single-trajectory while r is unchanged (~0.50): the gain is in **magnitude, not ranking**. Residual decomposes into a ~+1.3 kcal/mol systematic over-prediction plus ~2.4 kcal/mol scatter, and is **no longer large-cavity-specific** (errors spread across large-cavity/moderate/surface groups). Lone sign flip: S117V (в€’1.24 vs exp +0.9), a near-zero mutation. Absolute magnitudes remain approximate but now clear the revised thresholds.

> **NOTE вЂ” measured on the stripped-water path, which is the DEFAULT.** These numbers were
> produced with `ROSETTA_STRIP_WATERS=true` (strip). Strip was the default *until 2026-05-30*,
> was briefly switched to preserve (commit 3318bc9), and was **reverted to strip on 2026-05-31**
> as the validated, standard-Rosetta-practice baseline вЂ” so these panel numbers again describe
> the **default** path. **Preserve-waters** (`ROSETTA_STRIP_WATERS=False`) is now **opt-in**:
> it re-appends crystallographic HOH and is validated only on buried-water target **Barnase
> T26A** (strip в€’0.34 wrong-sign в†’ preserve +3.47 correct, exp +1.3; a **+3.80 shift**, 216 HOH
> confirmed reaching the pose). Preserve is a documented Rosetta anti-pattern at the all-static
> level, and its **panel-level behaviour remains unmeasured**; the proper fix is selective
> buried-only / movable waters (Build Queue В§9). The panel's surface/cavity mutations are not
> near buried waters, so the opt-in preserve path would be unlikely to change these specific
> metrics вЂ” but that is **unconfirmed**.
