| `test_pyrosetta_convergence_diag.py` | 3 levels (3/5/8 relax cycles) Г— 5 trajectories вЂ” is large-cavity bias convergence-fixable or baked in |

Full pipeline validation script: `scripts/validate_full_pipeline.txt`

### Rosetta ddG methodology & known deviations

Context for the systematic over-prediction (panel mean signed error в‰€ +1.3 kcal/mol; e.g. L99A +7.95 vs exp +5.0). Three axes, two of them deliberate/known deviations from the canonical protocol:

1. **Basis вЂ” actual implementation (modeled on, but deviating from, canonical cartesian_ddg).** ddG is computed by a **manual symmetric-relax protocol** (`rosetta_bridge.py:1449-1464`), **not** the Rosetta `cartesian_ddg` application: clone the cache-relaxed WT в†’ `MutateResidue` в†’ **torsion-space `FastRelax`(mutant)**; **independently `FastRelax` a re-cloned WT**; subtract **full-pose `ref2015` total scores** в†’ `ddG = score(mut) в€’ score(WT_re-relax)`; **median over N trajectories**. It is **MODELED ON** the canonical `cartesian_ddg` / `ref2015_cart` protocol (Park 2016; Frenz 2020) but **DEVIATES**: it uses **plain `ref2015` in TORSION space with FastRelax** (`:1401`, `:1420`) вЂ” not `cartesian_ddg`, not `ref2015_cart`, not cartesian minimisation. **Only the multi-trajectory + median noise-smoothing mirrors** the canonical 3вЂ“5 round averaging. Consequence: the published **2.94 REUв†’kcal/mol calibration does NOT apply** (see Calibration item); magnitudes are reported as **raw, uncalibrated REU**. вљ  The stub docstring (`:1115`) and one `method_note` string (`:1654`) still say "CartesianDDG"/"ref2015_cart" вЂ” aspirational labels the running code has never matched; do not take them as the implemented protocol.

2. **Calibration (KNOWN LEVER вЂ” AUDIT COMPLETE 2026-05-30; VERDICT: leave uncalibrated).** ref2015 cartesian_ddg REU famously requires a **~2.94 scaling factor в†’ kcal/mol** (Park 2016), and that factor is **protocol-specific**. Audit verdict:
   - The active ddG path is **NOT `cartesian_ddg`**. It is the manual protocol above (`rosetta_bridge.py:1449-1464`): clone WT в†’ mutate в†’ `FastRelax`(mutant) в†’ independently `FastRelax` a re-cloned WT в†’ subtract full-pose `ref2015` total scores; median over trajectories. **`ref2015` TORSION space**, not `ref2015_cart`, not cartesian minimisation.
   - Reported **"kcal/mol" = raw `ref2015` REU delta, with NO conversion** (implicit factor **1.0**; grep confirms no `2.94` / scaling anywhere in `rosetta_bridge.py`, the worker, or `config.py`).
   - **Park's 2.94 does NOT apply** (different protocol *and* score function). Worked check on the 2LZM panel (`scripts/validate_2lzm_results.json`, whose `predicted_median` values are the raw REU deltas): Г·2.94 lowers MAE **2.59 в†’ 1.24** but **over-corrects** вЂ” the bias flips negative (mean signed error +1.28 в†’ в€’0.94) and the large-cavity mutations are wrecked (L99A 7.95в†’2.71 vs exp 5.0). So magnitudes are **genuinely UNCALIBRATED**, and the "ranking reliable / magnitudes approximate (~В±2.7 kcal/mol)" framing used elsewhere is **accurate, not a placeholder**. Scaling is **irrelevant to ranking/sign** (it is a monotonic transform).
   - **DECISION: do NOT add any scaling factor or fitted calibration.** 2.94 over-corrects, and a 10-point empirical fit would overfit. (Recorded explicitly so a future session does not add one.) If calibrated absolute magnitudes ever become a requirement, adopt the **canonical** `cartesian_ddg` (cartesian relax + `ref2015_cart` + averaging + 2.94) wholesale вЂ” see Build Queue backlog вЂ” rather than patching a factor onto the torsion-space delta.

3. **Water handling (KNOWN DEVIATION FROM BEST PRACTICE).** Established Rosetta practice is to **strip bulk/surface waters** вЂ” the implicit LazaridisвЂ“Karplus / `lk_ball` solvent term in `ref2015` already models surface desolvation вЂ” and keep **only buried/bridging structural waters**, and **not as static HOH records**: static waters act as immovable spheres and cause **clash-driven over-destabilization**. The supported **movable**-water approach is **Rosetta-ICO/ECO** (Pavlovicz, Park & DiMaio 2020). Our current default (`ROSETTA_STRIP_WATERS=False` в†’ **preserve ALL ~216 crystallographic waters, static**; commit 3318bc9) is a **deliberate deviation**: it fixes the buried-water case (**Barnase T26A validated**: strip в€’0.34 wrong-sign в†’ preserve +3.47 correct, exp +1.3) but is **expected to degrade non-buried surface/cavity mutations**. **DECISION PENDING:** after the preserve-path 2LZM re-validation (Build Queue В§9 item 1), reconsider the default вЂ” likely move to **selective buried-only** preservation, or revert the default to **strip** with preservation as opt-in.

### Cross-voter calibration benchmark вЂ” COMPLETE (2026-06-11, attended)

The diverse-protein calibration benchmark designed in В§9 has now **run to completion and been analyzed in an attended session** (Claude + user). It supersedes the В§9 dry-run *motivation* and turns the protocol + weighting questions from *status* into **benchmark-backed decisions**. **Evidence basis:** `cache/stability_datagen/benchmark_rows.jsonl` вЂ” **1373/1373 rows** (S669 669 / Ssym_dir 352 / Ssym_inv 352), 0 malformed, 1373 unique keys, lossless/deduped; **gitignored, NOT committed** (the analysis was attended, on a local artifact вЂ” these numbers are transcribed, not re-derivable from a committed file). The run was resumed after a Windows-Update auto-reboot вЂ” GPU was down post-reboot so ESM ran CPU-only (~13 h); **data unaffected** (deterministic 8M model, full coverage).

**Sign convention вЂ” VERIFIED empirically.** Positive = destabilizing across `exp_ddg` and all predictors. DynaMut2 single-mutant sign-normalization confirmed correct (positive correlations with rosetta/rasp/thermompnn).

**Accuracy on CLEAN scopes vs `exp_ddg`** (Pearson r / Spearman ПЃ / RMSE / sign-acc on |exp|>1):

| Voter | n | r | ПЃ | RMSE | sign | note |
|-------|--:|--:|--:|-----:|-----:|------|
| ThermoMPNN (clean) | 1252 | +0.65 | +0.66 | 1.49 | 0.87 | **best** |
| RaSP | 1316 | +0.47 | +0.51 | 1.78 | 0.75 | strong 2nd |
| Rosetta torsion | 200 | +0.29 | +0.37 | 4.83 | 0.72 | weak corr, poor magnitude |
| DynaMut2 | 42 | +0.34 | вЂ” | вЂ” | вЂ” | **CONTAMINATED вЂ” see flag** |
| Rosetta cartesian 1-cycle | 198 | в€’0.01 | вЂ” | 11.3 | 0.46 | **BROKEN** (median bias в€’4) |
| ESM-tolerance | 1373 | в€’0.04 | в€’0.13 | вЂ” | вЂ” | ~no ddG signal |
| CamSol | 1373 | в€’0.04 | вЂ” | вЂ” | вЂ” | different axis (solubility) |

Ranking confirmed head-to-head on the **same 176 mutations** (ThermoMPNN > RaSP > torsion > cart).

**Leakage confirmed.** ThermoMPNN training-provenance rows (n=95) inflate (r=0.73, RMSE=0.66) vs clean (r=0.65, RMSE=1.49) вЂ” contamination gating was necessary; the **clean number is the honest one**.

**Independence.** RaSP Г— ThermoMPNN **r=+0.71** (largely redundant); RaSP Г— Rosetta circular (RaSP trained on Rosetta labels); **Rosetta Г— ThermoMPNN r=+0.38 вЂ” the most independent pairing.**

**Agreement-as-confidence вЂ” holds, but WEAK.** When RaSP & ThermoMPNN agree (low spread), consensus error drops 34% (0.89 vs 1.35 kcal/mol) вЂ” but this is agreement between two *correlated* voters, so it is weak confirmation; **sign accuracy barely changes** with agreement.

**Calibration / bias.** Both ML voters compress magnitude (regression slope в‰€0.31 vs exp в†’ predict в‰€в…“ of true ddG: good for **ranking**, miscalibrated for **absolute magnitude**). Rosetta torsion slope 0.78 (better-scaled magnitude, but noisier). **Per-protein offset sd 1.1вЂ“1.6 kcal/mol for all three в†’ bias is NOT reproducible across proteins; a single global correction won't fix it** вЂ” confirms the В§9 "calibratable = reproduces across proteins" test fails here (carry the per-protein range, don't globally calibrate).

**Anti-symmetry** (reconstructed 349/352 Ssym pairs; validated by exp showing r(dir,в€’inv)=+1.000, sum=0.000): ThermoMPNN moderately anti-symmetric (r=0.70) but forward+reverse **sum to +0.70** (destabilization bias); RaSP weak (r=0.30), sum **+1.64**. Both ML voters lean destabilizing **regardless of direction** в†’ **least reliable on STABILIZING mutations**. ESM & CamSol come out symmetric (non-directional), confirming they are **not** ddG predictors.

**RESOLVED вЂ” PROTOCOL = TORSION.** Torsion-space `ref2015` FastRelax **stays the deployed Rosetta ddG protocol**. The fast **1-cycle** cartesian arm is **unusable** (rв‰€0, sign 0.46, RMSE 11, в‰€в€’4 magnitude bias). **CAVEAT (explicit, permanent):** the 1-cycle verdict above is on the **CHEAP 1-CYCLE cartesian**, NOT full multi-cycle `cartesian_ddg`. **UPDATE 2026-06-12 вЂ” multi-cycle diagnostic COMPLETE (В§9), and it REINFORCES protocol=torsion.** CC ran cartesian at **3 AND 5 cycles** on a clean 24-mutation apples-to-apples subset (2LZM/2WQG/2HBB): on the clean 2LZM anchor cart-5 out-ranks torsion (r 0.781 vs 0.611) вЂ” genuine ranking signal вЂ” **but it is NOT converged by 5 cycles** (cart5~cart3 r ~0.5, ~3 REU still moving), its magnitude/bias is cycle-dependent, and the mini-proteins + the stabilizer tail do not refine; attended DECISION (Claude + user) = **stay torsion** (non-convergence + cost + no generalization; see В§9). **Refined reading:** *"cartesian is broken"* is more precisely **"cartesian breaks on hard/clash-prone proteins; on clean folds it carries genuine but UNCONVERGED ranking signal"** (the hard proteins were not tested by the diagnostic). This revises the item-2 *"leave uncalibrated"* status above into a **benchmark-backed decision**: torsion's slope-0.78 magnitude is the best available, still uncalibrated, and neither the 1-cycle nor the (unconverged) multi-cycle cartesian improves it.

**DynaMut2 вЂ” accuracy UNVERIFIED by this benchmark.** All 42 DynaMut2 rows are training/unknown provenance (**zero clean**), **S669-only** (no Ssym coverage), n=42; the +0.34 is on contaminated data and may be **inflated**. Its single-mutant **sign** is confirmed (above), but **accuracy needs clean eval data**. The `DYNAMUT2_MM_SIGN_VERIFIED` (multi-mutant) flag is **UNAFFECTED** вЂ” a different code path, not tested here; it remains inferred-not-verified (see В§4).

---

## 8. Known Issues and Technical Debt

### From `scripts/rosetta_validation_notes.md` (PyRosetta protocol audit)

| Issue | Severity | Detail |
|-------|----------|--------|
| Single relax trajectory | вљ пёЏ Medium | 1 trajectory per mutation; adds ~1вЂ“2 kcal/mol stochastic noise; RMSE 5.49 in benchmark |
| cleanATOM removes crystallographic waters | вљ пёЏ High | Causes wrong-sign predictions for T26A (Barnase) and G88V (SNase) where buried waters contribute to stability; **one-line fix: preserve HOH records** |
| Cavity-filling mutation overestimation | вљ пёЏ High | A98V: +14.52 predicted vs в€’0.5 experimental; single trajectory can't resolve backbone strain for volume-increasing substitutions; fix: detect mutant > WT size, use more relax cycles |
| No large backbone flexibility | вљ пёЏ Medium | FastRelax can't model local unfolding; proline-insertion destabilisation underestimated |
| Single-chain scoring for oligomers | вљ пёЏ Low | 1HSG chains A+B both loaded; interface contacts from B on A mutations present but not explicitly managed |

### PyRosetta ddG benchmark failure modes (from run 1)

**Failure mode 1 вЂ” Systematic overestimation of destabilisation:**
I88V (+5.264 vs +0.6), L69A (+6.6 vs +2.4), L99A (+7.137 vs +4.0), A98V (+14.52 vs в€’0.5). Root cause: single trajectory landing in poor local minimum. **Quantified 2026-05-29** (aggregation diagnostic): per-trajectory spread в‰€ **8 kcal/mol** (two-sided), and **median** is the best aggregator (MAE 2.79 < mean 3.51 < min 3.84) вЂ” MIN is refuted. The convergence diagnostic (2026-05-29) showed more relax cycles also reduce the *bias* (not just noise) вЂ” **partially**: at 8+8 cycles ~half the gap closes (L99A +9.24в†’+7.30, V87M +7.24в†’+5.37) and spread drops 7.61в†’5.13 kcal/mol, but magnitudes do not fully calibrate (V87M retains residual bias). Fix path: multi-trajectory **median** aggregation **+ more relax cycles for a validation tier**; absolute magnitudes stay approximate until a full re-run confirms RMSE.

**Failure mode 2 вЂ” Wrong sign on buried mutations:**
T26A (в€’2.437 predicted vs +1.3 exp), G88V (в€’0.25 vs +2.1), V82A (в€’0.06 vs +1.75). Root cause: `cleanATOM` removing crystallographic waters that stabilise buried positions in Barnase and SNase.

### Revised benchmark thresholds (updated based on run 1)
Realistic thresholds for the current single-trajectory protocol: `r > 0.30`, `RMSE < 4.00`, `sign_accuracy в‰Ґ 60%`. **DONE 2026-05-31** вЂ” `test_rosetta_benchmark.py` re-scoped for honesty: the aggregate correlation test (`test_benchmark_correlation_acceptable`) is now THE gate at these thresholds (with a `MIN_BENCHMARK_ENTRIES=6` minimum-N guard that **skips, not fails**, below the floor); per-mutation tests only **record** to `benchmark_results.json` and assert **sign only** for `|experimental| > 1.5` (`SIGN_ASSERT_MIN_ABS_EXP`), never magnitude (the old В±2.0 kcal/mol tolerance gated on stochastic single-trajectory noise вЂ” T26A came back +1.41 vs +7.74 across two live runs). Also fixed the cp1252 `UnicodeEncodeError` (the `вњ“`/`вњ—` summary glyph в†’ ASCII `[PASS]`/`[FAIL]` + best-effort UTF-8 stream reconfigure). Module still SKIPS cleanly (all 12 tests) without WSL2/PyRosetta. **Follow-up (also 2026-05-31, commit after 06f6478):** (a) **xfail buckets** вЂ” buried В§8-failure-mode-2 wrong-sign cases under the default strip-water path (G88V, V82A) are now `@pytest.mark.xfail(strict=False, raises=AssertionError)` so a correct sign on the default path is an expected-failure, not a deterministic RED; T26A stays bucket-1 (record-only) since `|exp|=1.3 в‰¤ 1.5`; (b) **opt-in gate** вЂ” live run now requires `STRUCTUREBOT_RUN_LIVE_BENCHMARK=1` AND WSL2 AND PyRosetta (short-circuit `and`), so a dev box with PyRosetta installed no longer launches the hours-long suite by accident.

### ColabFold accuracy benchmark (regression guard, NOT an accuracy claim)
`tests/test_colabfold_benchmark.py` (DONE 2026-06-01) folds a small panel of well-characterized monomers (**1CRN** ~46, **1UBQ** ~76, **1PGB**/GB1 ~56, **2LZM** ~164) via the ColabFold bridge (default 5 models / 3 recycles; result + JAX compile caches keep it from being fully cold) and measures **predicted-vs-native all-pairs CО± RMSD** (headless, BioPython `SVDSuperimposer`) + mean pLDDT. **Honesty pattern mirrors the rosetta benchmark exactly**: SKIP BY DEFAULT (live only on `STRUCTUREBOT_RUN_LIVE_COLABFOLD=1` + env; CI collects + skips, 0 folds); per-protein results are **RECORDED**, the gate is on **panel medians** (`median RMSD < 3.0 Г…`, `median pLDDT > 70`, **no fold ran on CPU** вЂ” silent GPUв†’CPU fallback is a real failure mode) with a `MIN_BENCHMARK_ENTRIES=3` guard that **skips, not fails**, below the floor. Thresholds are **deliberately generous regression guards** вЂ” AF2 nails these (sub-Г… to ~1.5 Г…) so the gate catches pipeline breakage (wrong chain, parse bug, CPU fallback, MSA failure), not accuracy frontiers. Results JSON: `scripts/colabfold_benchmark_results.json`. A small additive `gpu_used` field was added to the ColabFold bridge result (parsed from the worker log) to power the CPU-fallback check.

### вњ… ColabFold DEFAULT (5-model) fold вЂ” RESOLVED via XLA on-demand allocator (2026-06-01)
**Error reporting FIXED** (commit `83a27a8`, merged to `main`): the worker previously did `error = log[-3000:]` on `stdout+stderr` concatenated, so a benign trailing TF/oneDNN stderr line buried the real traceback; now it surfaces the last 60 lines of **stdout AND stderr separately labelled** (+ `returncode`, `stdout_tail`, `stderr_tail`) and the bridge propagates it (no 300-char clip). Canonical formatter `_format_worker_failure()` + 3 unit tests.

**Root cause (diagnosed with the now-visible error):** the default 5-model/3-recycle fold (and ANY config beyond the `quick` 1/1 preset) **SIGSEGV'd (exit -11)** вЂ” XLA's **BFC GPU client preallocated ~48 GiB of pinned HOST memory** (в‰€ 4Г— the 12 GB VRAM, a staging pool, NOT a real need for a tiny fold), backed off 48в†’16 GiB, but **WSL2 caps at ~15 GiB** (default ~50% of the 31.7 GB host; no `~/.wslconfig`) в†’ every retry exceeded the cap в†’ segfault. Isolation: 5-model/1-recycle FAILED and 1-model/3-recycle FAILED (neither knob alone). **NOT a bridge bug** (args correct).

**FIX APPLIED (option 2 вЂ” XLA flag, no env/default change):** the worker now sets, for the `colabfold_batch` subprocess (alongside the JAX compile-cache env, via `os.environ.setdefault` so a user can override): `XLA_PYTHON_CLIENT_PREALLOCATE=false` and **`XLA_PYTHON_CLIENT_ALLOCATOR=platform`**. The `platform` allocator allocates GPU/host memory **on demand** instead of the BFC pool's giant upfront pinned-host preallocation. **Live-confirmed**: default 5-model/3-recycle **crambin (1CRN)** now completes **on GPU** (NOT CPU fallback), **no pinned-host request / no segfault**, **peak host RSS ~2.6 GiB** (vs the old 48 GiB demand), mean pLDDT 93.1 / pTM 0.68 вЂ” and it did NOT relocate the OOM to the 12 GB VRAM (the fold ran to completion on-device). Default mode now works within current WSL2 memory; the only remaining ceiling is the real GPU-VRAM limit on large/oligomer folds, which is what the `COLABFOLD_MAX_TOTAL_RESIDUES` budget guard exists for.

disulfide_bridge.py already enumerates inter-chain pairs). **Phase 2 (LATER, advanced redesign):** MPNN redesign at interface, salt-bridge scan on full complex, flex_ddG dual-state filter, CamSol/ColabFold re-validation.

**Completed (2026-06-07):** вњ… **Biological-assembly generation** (`bio_assembly` intent route + `_run_bio_assembly` thin orchestrator + AU mismatch detector + verb-guard 3a + correction-loop 3b): on "open as tetramer/dimer/oligomer", "generate biological assembly", "build the biological unit", etc. в†’ emits `sym #{model_id} assembly {assembly_id} copies true` on the ALREADY-LOADED model (never re-opens the structure, no duplicate model); default assembly=1, explicit override parsed; error-first lists available assemblies (`sym #N` bare) on failure; AU model hidden (not deleted), assembly group tracked in `session_state.generated_assemblies`. **On open:** AU-vs-biological mismatch detector compares loaded chain count against `n_subunits` from RCSB and surfaces a yellow advisory when biological > loaded (informational only вЂ” not auto-applied). **Guard fixes (3a):** `probe_chimerax_verbs()` wired into `main._handle_request` before `translate()` so Tier 2 of `_validate_command_verbs` fires in production (was never called before вЂ” root cause); `_HALLUCINATED_VERB_DENYLIST` trimmed back to the 10 original common-English-word entries (StructureBot tool names removed вЂ” the registry generalises to ANY unknown verb without enumeration; `assembly_analyser`, `tetramer_builder`, and any other novel verb are all caught by Tier 2). **Guard fixes (3b):** correction loop extracts the leading verb of `failed_cmd` and `fix_cmds[0]`; if they match AND the verb is not in the safe standard set в†’ halt with "Correction re-proposed the same non-existent verb". 32 tests; live-verified on 2VNC (see В§7). **This UNBLOCKS the interface-stabilization workflow** (double-mutant / mutation-scan on assembly interfaces, `assembly_analyser` zone-select on the full quaternary structure) вЂ” previously impossible because the full assembly wasn't available as a ChimeraX model. See В§3/В§6/В§7.

**вњ… DONE вЂ” ProteinMPNN constraint/scope honoured end-to-end** (2026-06-03; В§9 Priority-3a behavioural half). Made the Accuracy-scorer checks pass END-TO-END for a correct request. **Mapping table (NL в†’ translator field в†’ bridge в†’ ProteinMPNN flag):**

| NL pattern | translator `tool_inputs` | `_run_proteinmpnn` в†’ `analyze`/`_resolve` | ProteinMPNN flag |
|---|---|---|---|
| "chain A" | `chain`/`chain_id` | `chain_id` | `--chain_id` |
| "residues 20-30" | `design_positions:[20..30]` (+`design_scope:"selected"`) | designable set в†’ fix the complement | `--fixed_positions_jsonl` |
| "the selected residues" | `design_scope:"selected"` | live ChimeraX selection в†’ `design_positions`; else interface | `--fixed_positions_jsonl` |
| "redesign the interface" / "interface with chain B" | `design_scope:"interface"` (+`partner_chain`) | `interface_design` в†’ `compute_interface_positions` (BioPython) | `--fixed_positions_jsonl` |
| "no cysteines" / "no prolines" | `exclude_amino_acids:["C"]`/`["P"]` | `omit_aas` | `--omit_AAs` |
| "more soluble" / "hydrophilic" / "reduce aggregation" | `bias_amino_acids:[D E N Q H K R S T]` **or** `bias_toward:"soluble"` | `bias_aas` = polar/charged set | `--bias_AA_jsonl` (+weight 1.5) |

**Fixes:** (1) `bias_toward:"soluble"`/"solub"/"polar"/"aggregation" now maps to the hydrophilic bias вЂ” previously only the literal "hydrophil" matched, so the corpus's own "soluble" wording was **silently dropped**. (2) Prompt now instructs `design_positions` (EXPANDED integer list) for explicit ranges like "residues 20-30", which were previously unrepresentable (only `design_scope:"selected"` existed for live selections). **Already-correct (verified, not changed):** a restricted design that resolves to nothing **ERRORS** (no whole-chain fallback); an interface request without a live selection falls back to the deterministic BioPython interface computation; native cysteines are held fixed. **Live-validated on the real 1IL8 dimer:** interface-only design в†’ 21 designable positions (NOT the whole 71-residue chain), `omit_AAs="C"`, all 4 native Cys (7/9/34/50) held fixed; explicit scope 10-20 в†’ 11 designable. CI mocks the subprocess; the resolver runs on a real mini-PDB fixture. +10 tests (`test_proteinmpnn_constraints.py`). See В§6.

**вњ… DONE вЂ” Intent-override precedence audit + pinned test matrix** (2026-06-03, `tool_router.route()`). **Audit verdict: the documented В§2 override ORDER was correct** (validate_design first, then validate_ddg в†’ colabfold в†’ proline в†’ mpnn_esmfold в†’ glycan_positions в†’ netnglyc в†’ glycan в†’ salt_bridge в†’ cavity в†’ double_mutant в†’ mutation_scan) вЂ” **no ordering was changed.** Two correctness FIXES (not reorderings): **(1) precedence LOCK (`_claimed`)** вЂ” each full-replace override previously guarded only on its OWN tool's absence, so a LOWER-precedence override could clobber a HIGHER one on a dual-intent prompt (the documented order was *violable*); now the first/highest override to fire is the deterministic winner. **(2) `mutation_scan` fallback SCOPING** вЂ” it now only **upgrades a generic (`chimerax`) or `cavity` mis-route**; it can no longer clobber a specialized tool the translator chose. This fixes a real distractor-capture bug: **"CamSol *solubility scan*"** was being hijacked to `mutation_scan` (the keyword "solubility scan" matched), and a `proteinmpnn` redesign mentioning "improve solubility"/"reduce aggregation" was at risk of the same. +23 pinned tests (`test_router_precedence.py`); full suite green. See В§6.

| 1 | **Redundant ddG / stabilization ensemble** (ThermoMPNN вњ… В· RaSP вњ… В· DynaMut2 вњ… 2026-06-10 вЂ” **all 4 ddG axes IN**; calibration **benchmark вњ… COMPLETE 2026-06-11 в†’ see В§7 + the benchmark-backed weighting LOGIC**; next = exporter + aggregate) | **ALL FOUR ddG AXES NOW LANDED** вЂ” PHYSICS (Rosetta real / RaSP proxy, per-candidate handoff), ML/STATIC (ThermoMPNN), DYNAMICS (DynaMut2, independent) + the property axes (CamSol solubility, ESM fitness), all on one **lossless author-resnum-keyed record**.  **вњ… DynaMut2 вЂ” DONE (2026-06-10)** (`_run_dynamut2`; dynamics-axis shortlist/round-2 voter on the deep set, capped, concurrent with Rosetta; INDEPENDENT вЂ” never handed off; sign-normalised via the shared `normalize_dynamut2_ddg`, which ALSO fixed a pre-existing inverted-sign bug in the single + double-mutant paths вЂ” see В§13; empirical fallbacks excluded; 15 tests; live-verified all-4-axes + sign + API-failure-graceful).  **NEXT PHASE (the natural one now that the substrate is complete):** the **exporter** (one row per candidate, all axes) + the **cross-layer aggregate confidence** + the **weight-calibrating BENCHMARK** that sets RASP/THERMOMPNN/DYNAMUT2 weights from correlation-with-experiment per the В§9 aggregate-weighting spec (independence Г— confidence; note DynaMut2/ThermoMPNN share experimental supervision в†’ partial correlation; RaSP/ESM share structural context).  **cartesian_ddg** (Backlog, calibrated-magnitude) + **ThermoMPNN-D** (double mutants) remain later. Then **cartesian_ddg** (Backlog, calibrated-magnitude). **THEN the exporter + cross-layer aggregate + the BENCHMARK that calibrates the В§9 aggregate-weighting (independence Г— confidence, staged by round) вЂ” which sets RASP_WEIGHT/THERMOMPNN_WEIGHT etc. from correlation-with-experiment (proxy < real; account for ThermoMPNN/ESM redundancy).** Independence axes so far: PHYSICS (Rosetta real OR RaSP proxy вЂ” one slot), ML/STATIC (ThermoMPNN), + property axes CamSol/ESM; DYNAMICS (DynaMut2) enters next. **ThermoMPNN-D** (double mutants) = later. **Validate each new voter on a trusted case (2LZM panel) before trusting.** **KNOWN LIMITATION (RaSP):** insertion-coded chains (antibody Kabat/IMGT вЂ” Fabs/scFvs) get NO RaSP physics-proxy вЂ” pdbfixer strips icodes в†’ alignment length-diverges в†’ whole-chain not_computed (safe, not mis-attributed; ThermoMPNN+Rosetta still cover). Matters for CHO/HEK biologics/antibody work; candidate refinement = an icode-preserving clean step. See В§4. |
| 1 | **Mammalian (CHO/HEK) developability / expressibility proxy layer** | Expression interest is **CHO/HEK, not E. coli** вЂ” and there is **no open-source drop-in mammalian-titer predictor** (NetSolP/SoluProt are E. coli-specific; mammalian expression is secretory-pathway-dominated: signal peptide в†’ ER folding в†’ glycosylation в†’ secretion). So **assemble a composite developability score from transferable proxies вЂ” 3 of 4 already built**: **aggregation propensity** (the net-new piece вЂ” AGGRESCAN3D open-source standalone, OR Spatial Aggregation Propensity in the existing WSL2 PyRosetta); **intrinsic solubility** (`camsol_bridge`, organism-agnostic вЂ” have); **fold stability/Tm** (the ddG ensemble above вЂ” building; a stable fold is one of the strongest levers on mammalian secretability); **N-glycosylation** (`glycan_bridge` вЂ” have; central to ER folding/secretion). Optional **SignalP 6.0** (open source) for secreted constructs. Converges with the stabilization work вЂ” same machinery serves both. Verify AGGRESCAN3D's current standalone/license status before wiring |
| 1 | ~~**Deep-tier coverage: GRID vs SHORTLIST**~~ вњ… **RESOLVED 2026-06-09** | Decision: **FULL grid is the default** (max data вЂ” the user's bias; safe because Rosetta is opt-in + the estimate is honest); **shortlist (top-K by fast score) is an explicit opt-in** offered with its own estimate whenever the full-grid estimate is expensive. Shortlist **never silently drops** вЂ” deferred candidates are RETAINED as `not_computed`. `ROSETTA_SHORTLIST_K`=15. Built + live-verified (full в‰€2.1 h vs shortlist top-15 в‰€39 min on 2HHB) |
| 1 | ~~**Symmetric vs asymmetric ddG**~~ вњ… **RESOLVED 2026-06-09** | Decision: **symmetric (paired WT re-relax) stays the default** (the variance-reduced, higher-quality ddG); **asymmetric is an explicit opt-in** ("asymmetric" вЂ” single cached-WT reference, ~2Г— faster, noisier), always **labelled** in output, never mixed within a scan. `ROSETTA_DDG_BASIS`=symmetric. Built + live-verified |
| 1 | **Excel export + cross-layer aggregate scoring** (NEXT вЂ” the lossless result model is now its substrate) | The scan result is now LOSSLESS (every candidate keyed by (chain,pos,wt,mut) with camsol/esm/ddg/ddg_basis/ddg_source/tier/fast_score/combined_score, `not_computed` where a tier didn't run). NEXT: (a) a clean serialization to Excel/CSV (one row per candidate, all measures); (b) **cross-layer aggregate scoring** joining future voters (ThermoMPNN/RaSP) on the same candidate key в†’ the evidence-rich, per-source-transparent, agreement-based aggregate-confidence direction (В§9 Strategic direction). ### Validate-design meta-tool вЂ” agreed design (DONE вЂ” kept for reference)

A **thin orchestrator** (a `tool_router` dispatch + result-assembly method, **not** a new bridge вЂ” it composes existing bridges). Inputs: a designed sequence (or a reused in-session ColabFold result) + a reference structure. Three evidence sources:

1. **ColabFold** вЂ” fold confidence (mean/per-residue pLDDT, pTM/ipTM, PAE). **Reuse an existing in-session `colabfold_results` fold instead of re-folding** when one matches; only fold if absent.
2. **ChimeraX matchmaker** вЂ” superpose the predicted model onto the reference; report RMSD (+ aligned-residue count).
3. **Rosetta** вЂ” FastRelax + `ref2015` total energy of the predicted model.

**Energy-reporting rule (important):**
- **Default = clash-free / low-energy SANITY check** вЂ” report the relaxed total energy as a "structure is physically reasonable / not clashing" signal, NOT a stability claim.
- **Like-for-like RELATIVE score** (design vs reference О”energy) **only when topologies match** (matchmaker RMSD low / same fold) **or on explicit request**.
- **DECLINE a cross-topology absolute stability number** and **state why** (ref2015 deltas across different folds are not comparable; our ddG path is uncalibrated вЂ” see В§7). Surface the sanity signal instead.

**Reports are EVIDENCE-RICH:** surface ALL underlying outputs (pLDDT map, PAE, RMSD, per-term energies, the per-source warnings) rather than collapsing to a verdict; the **interpretive natural-language summary is DEFERRED** to a later iteration. Mirrors the existing error-first / `ToolStepResult` + viz idiom; no new venv or external dependency.

### Backlog

| Item | Rationale |
|------|-----------|
| **Confirmation surfaces вЂ” echo-back + interactive sequence window** (PROPOSED, design doc: `CONFIRMATION_SURFACES_PROPOSAL.md`) | Give the user verifiable/correctable views of what the translator is about to do / has done, so the eval's failure modes (wrong chain, off-by-one range, resnumв‰ seq-position, ambiguous interpretation) are caught + overridable at the point of use. **(A) Echo-back**: a new `interpretation`/`interpreted_action` schema field (both backends) + a deterministic **faithfulness guard** (summary в†” emitted command chain/range/distance/tool; unfaithful = a defect, flag + confidence-downgrade, never overrides the command). **(B) Sequence window**: the live selection read back from ChimeraX ground truth (`info residues sel`, auth IDs) in the **native Sequence Viewer**, bidirectional + editable в†’ `session.selection`. Principles: ambient over modal; tier the gate to reversibility; read-back from ground truth, never the LLM's claim. **Out-of-eval guardrail** (the override path must never feed a scored translation). Phasing: echo-back first (schema + guard, sequences AFTER in-flight translator changes / the baseline run), sequence window second. Build NOTHING until reviewed |
| **Selective / movable buried-only water handling** (Rosetta-ECO) | Real fix for the water trade-off: keep **only buried/bridging** waters (the `ref2015` `lk_ball` implicit solvent already models surface desolvation) and treat them as **movable** (Rosetta-ICO/ECO; Pavlovicz, Park & DiMaio 2020) вЂ” captures the T26A buried-water benefit without the surface-mutation penalty that preserve-all-static causes. Canonical cartesian adoption remains gated on **solving convergence first** (extend cycles + test the hard proteins) |

| **Mid-execution ESC / cancellation** | Long-running tools (PyRosetta ~15 min, ColabFold ~5 min) have no cancellation; needs a background-thread pattern |

### Strategic direction (post-capability) вЂ” evidence-rich multi-tool analysis + aggregate confidence

Once the near-term capability tranche lands (ddG ensemble, mammalian developability layer,
RFdiffusion), focus SHIFTS from breadth (more tools) to **output quality and utility**. North
star: for any engineering question, run the relevant tools, **document each tool's output
side-by-side, and compute an aggregate score with an explicit confidence** вЂ” so the user sees
both the consensus AND the disagreement, never a single opaque number.

This GENERALIZES the validate-design meta-tool's existing idiom ("Reports are EVIDENCE-RICH:
surface ALL underlying outputs rather than collapsing to a verdict") across the whole suite.
The redundant-ddG ensemble (Priority 1) is the first concrete instance: N independent О”О”G
predictors + the ESM evolutionary voter, each shown, ranked by agreement, with an aggregate
confidence that is HIGH when voters concur and LOW when they split.

**Design principles (to codify when this phase opens):**
- **Per-source transparency** вЂ” every contributing tool's raw output is shown and attributed;
  the aggregate never hides a dissenting source.
- **Confidence from agreement, not assertion** вЂ” aggregate confidence derives from inter-tool
  concordance (plus each tool's own confidence where it reports one, e.g. the `ddg_spread`/
  `ddg_confidence` already in `mutation_scanner`), never a flat claim.
- **Honest disagreement** вЂ” when sources conflict (ThermoMPNN stabilizing vs Rosetta
  destabilizing), SURFACE the split and downgrade confidence rather than pick a winner. Mirrors
  the validate-design "DECLINE + state why" honesty rule.
- **Error-first / `ToolStepResult` reuse** вЂ” a failed/absent voter drops out with a note and
  degrades the aggregate gracefully; it never breaks the analysis.
- **One shared report assembler** вЂ” a thin orchestrator (NOT a new bridge) so every analysis
  (stabilization, developability, design-validation) emits the same evidence-rich +
  aggregate-confidence shape.

This phase is also the natural home for the interpretive natural-language summary deferred from
validate-design v1 and the confirmation-surfaces echo-back (Backlog) вЂ” all of it is "make the
outputs trustworthy and legible" work.

### Aggregate ddG weighting вЂ” independence Г— confidence, staged by round

> **FORWARD SPEC for the not-yet-built aggregate layer. Do NOT implement raw numbers from this.** The
> benchmark (2026-06-11, В§7) has now **replaced the placeholder weights with benchmark-backed two-tier
> LOGIC** (see "Calibrated weighting LOGIC" at the end of this subsection). The independence-axis +
> staged-by-round framing below is **confirmed by the benchmark** and reconciles with the
> mutation_scanner fast-tier/deep-tier triageв†’validate design (В§3). **Weights remain LOGIC, not fitted
> coefficients** вЂ” a regularized fit on the clean overlap is a future option, not done.

Each source's weight = **(diversity allocation to its independence axis) Г— (confidence of the
estimator filling it)**. Two distinct reasons to up/down-weight, both applied:
- **INDEPENDENCE:** correlated sources don't double-vote. RaSP and Rosetta are ONE physics axis
  (RaSP is a trained Rosetta surrogate) вЂ” never both at once.
- **CONFIDENCE:** a more reliable estimator carries more of its axis's weight. Rosetta > RaSP is
  principled, not a preference вЂ” a surrogate can't be more accurate than what it approximates.

**Independence axes (stability; corroborate в†’ agreement feeds confidence):**
- **PHYSICS** вЂ” RaSP (proxy, low confidence) OR Rosetta (real, high confidence); handoff per candidate.
- **ML / STATIC** вЂ” ThermoMPNN.
- **DYNAMICS** вЂ” DynaMut2 (most differentiated).

**Property axes (integrated, not corroborated):** CamSol (solubility), ESM (fitness).

**Staged by round (driven by what's dense/cheap vs sparse/expensive):**
- **ROUND 1 вЂ” dense, local:** RaSP + ThermoMPNN (+ CamSol, ESM). DynaMut2 absent (remote API,
  can't be dense). Physics (RaSP) weighted LOW (proxy). Two stability axes.
- **ROUND 2 вЂ” shortlist / opt-in:** Rosetta + ThermoMPNN + DynaMut2 (+ properties). RaSP в†’ 0
  (handoff); physics (Rosetta) weighted HIGHER (confidence); dynamics axis enters. Three stability
  axes вЂ” more diverse AND more confident.

Per candidate, **renormalise over present axes (sum to 1)**. RaSP is RETAINED even when zeroed вЂ”
the **RaSP в€’ Rosetta delta is a proxy-QC signal, not corroboration**.

**Calibrated weighting LOGIC (benchmark-backed 2026-06-11, В§7 вЂ” LOGIC, NOT fitted numbers).** The
benchmark measured the independence + confidence factors directly. Record them as *logic*, because
Rosetta n=200 is too thin to fit tight coefficients without overfitting (a regularized weight-fit on
the clean overlap is a future option if explicit numbers are ever wanted вЂ” do **not** write precise
weights as if calibrated):
- **Fast full-coverage triage (RANK everything): ThermoMPNN + RaSP.** Best (r 0.65) + strong-2nd
  (r 0.47), both dense/cheap. Their agreement is **corroboration between correlated voters**
  (r=+0.71) with **shared blind spots** вЂ” magnitude compression (slope в‰€0.31) **and** a
  stabilizing-mutation bias (anti-symmetry sums +0.70 / +1.64). So it is a strong **ranking** filter
  but only **modest** confidence: count the ML pair as **~1.5 votes, not 2** (redundancy + the
  RaSP-vs-Rosetta circularity, RaSP being trained on Rosetta labels).
- **Deep / selected subset (CONFIRM): ThermoMPNN + Rosetta** вЂ” the **complementary, non-redundant**
  pair (cross-correlation only +0.38, the most independent). Use ML for **ranking**, Rosetta (torsion,
  slope 0.78) for **magnitude calibration** + an **independent sign check on exactly the stabilizing
  calls the ML pair is worst at**. Matches the existing fast-tierв†’deep-tier triageв†’validate design (В§3).
- **DynaMut2** вЂ” a dynamics-axis **EXTRA**, accuracy **UNVERIFIED** here (contaminated subset, В§7 flag).
  Optional; **do not anchor** to it.
- **ESM-tolerance + CamSol** вЂ” **OFF the ddG/stability axis** (both rв‰€в€’0.04 to exp; symmetric under
  anti-symmetry). CamSol = solubility/developability axis; ESM-tolerance = fitness/variant-tolerance
  flag. (Reconciles with the property-axis framing above and В§3 вЂ” integrated, never folded into the
  stability vote.)

Per candidate, **renormalise over present axes (sum to 1)**. RaSP is RETAINED even when zeroed вЂ”
the **RaSP в€’ Rosetta delta is a proxy-QC signal, not corroboration**.

(Today's `present_voters_score` already renormalises over present voters вЂ” the per-candidate,
sum-to-1 substrate this spec extends; ThermoMPNN is the ML/STATIC axis, already wired.)

### Stability-Model Calibration & Validation Benchmark вЂ” вњ… COMPLETE (2026-06-11), results recorded in В§7

> **вњ… BENCHMARK COMPLETE + ATTENDED ANALYSIS DONE (2026-06-11).** The diverse-protein run executed to
> completion and was analyzed in an attended session. **The headline results live in В§7 ("Cross-voter
> calibration benchmark вЂ” COMPLETE")**; this subsection is kept as the design/method-of-record and now
> points to them. **Evidence basis:** `cache/stability_datagen/benchmark_rows.jsonl` вЂ” **1373/1373 rows**
> (S669 669 / Ssym_dir 352 / Ssym_inv 352), 0 malformed, 1373 unique keys, lossless/deduped; **gitignored,
> NOT committed** (attended analysis on a local artifact). Resumed after a Windows-Update auto-reboot в†’
> GPU down в†’ ESM CPU-only (~13 h), data unaffected.
>
> **What it resolved:** (1) the six designed outputs below were all produced (per-voter confidence,
> cross-voter independence, agreement-as-confidence premise, per-voter bias, anti-symmetry at scale,
> weighting); (2) the weighting placeholders above are replaced by **benchmark-backed two-tier LOGIC**
> (NOT fitted numbers вЂ” Rosetta n=200 is too thin to fit tight coefficients; a regularized weight-fit on
> the clean overlap stays a future option); (3) **PROTOCOL = TORSION** (the 1-cycle cartesian arm is
> broken вЂ” see В§7); (4) DynaMut2 accuracy is **unverified** here (contaminated subset). **The earlier
> 917-row dry-run paragraph below is now historical** (superseded by the 1373-row benchmark in В§7).
>
> **Superseded design-note (2026-06-10, historical):** the Part-2 data-generation harness
> (`scripts/stability_datagen.py`, `a6c7bc2`/`75d396f`) first ran on a 917-row dry-run set
> (`cache/stability_datagen/rows.jsonl`, 1PGA-dominated + T4L) вЂ” *collection only*, recorded below as
> the motivation that drove the diverse-set design. The benchmark proper has since run (above).

**Purpose.** One diverse-protein run that produces, from the same data, six outputs:
1. **Per-voter confidence** вЂ” leakage-controlled, outlier-robust correlation vs experiment.
2. **Cross-voter independence** вЂ” pairwise correlation structure, to validate the В§9 axes empirically.
3. **Agreement-as-confidence premise validation** вЂ” cross-voter spread vs error vs experiment.
4. **Per-voter bias** вЂ” offset + slope and their cross-protein reproducibility.
5. **Anti-symmetry at scale** вЂ” Ssym fwd/rev.
6. **Calibrated weights** вЂ” В§9 independence Г— confidence, resolving the provisional placeholders.

**Design principles (hard-won).**
- **Diversity over volume.** The calibration set's value is protein diversity and
  training-disjointness, NOT row count. Many proteins from disjoint training distributions beat
  thousands of rows from a voter's training set. (See dry-run findings below вЂ” volume of the wrong
  data is the trap.)
- **Held-out is per-voter, not global.** Each voter has a different training set (ThermoMPNN в†’
  Tsuboyama mega-scale; DynaMut2 в†’ S2648/VariBench family; RaSP в†’ Rosetta ddG, so RaSP-vs-Rosetta is
  always circular; Rosetta в†’ physics, the leakage-free anchor). Score each voter only on ITS
  training-disjoint subset. **The per-voter provenance audit is the gating first step** вЂ” no analysis
  until each voter's evaluation subset is confirmed disjoint from its training.
- **"Calibratable" = reproduces across proteins.** Measure offset/slope PER protein; examine the
  spread. Tight spread в†’ stable systematic bias в†’ calibrate with pooled values (spread = the honest
  error bar). Wide spread в†’ protein-dependent bias в†’ a single global correction would misfire в†’ do
  NOT calibrate globally; carry the bias range and account for it instead.
- **Robust statistics mandatory.** Rosetta carries a clash tail (clash artifacts > +10, e.g.
  K50P в‰€ +97 REU vs experiment capped ~5). Use rank-based/robust methods; flag clash artifacts as
  low-confidence rather than treating them as real ddG.
- **Property axes characterized separately.** CamSol (solubility) and ESM (fitness) are NOT ddG; do
  not fold them into the stability correlation or the stability vote. Characterize on their own terms.
- **DynaMut2 stays subset-limited.** Remote API (~20вЂ“30 s/mut, capped) в†’ a smaller fixed diverse
  subset; it remains the least-powered voter.

**Dual output (the delivered artifact).** Every candidate carries **Raw/Unmodified ddG** (lossless
source of truth вЂ” never overwritten) AND **Calibrated ddG** (a derived view), for user
discrimination. The calibrated value is produced only at the aggregate/interpretation layer over the
lossless record, and carries: **provenance** (which dataset, the offset/slope applied), a **version
tag** (recalibration must not silently change old results), an **uncertainty** (from the
cross-protein spread), and an **out-of-distribution caveat** (a calibration fit on benchmark proteins
may not transfer to very different targets).

**Execution model вЂ” ATTENDED.** CC may compute the mechanical analysis (correlations,
spread-vs-error, bias decomposition, the provenance audit). The **judgment** вЂ” interpreting leakage
vs signal, deciding weights, accepting/refuting the premise, calibrate-or-not вЂ” is the attended
human+Claude step. **No autonomous weight-setting or in-pipeline calibration.**

**Dry-run findings (motivation, NOT results).** 917 rows, 1PGA-dominated + T4L; one protein,
ThermoMPNN-leakage-contaminated вЂ” recorded as the motivation for the design above, NOT as benchmark
results. **Provenance of these numbers:** the run lives at `cache/stability_datagen/rows.jsonl`
(917 rows) + a descriptive `SUMMARY.txt` (counts/ranges/medians only). The **raw rows and the
descriptive summary are the only saved artifacts**; the correlation / spread-vs-error / offset-slope
findings below were computed in-session and are **NOT independently saved** вЂ” re-derivable from
`rows.jsonl`, but currently unverified against an artifact:
- **Leakage trap demonstrated:** ThermoMPNN +0.83 vs exp (Protein G в‰€ its Tsuboyama training set);
  the 3-voter consensus (+0.785) "lost" to it вЂ” a naive read would wrongly say "drop the aggregate."
  This is why diversity + provenance audit are non-negotiable.
- **Premise holds directionally:** spreadв†’error Spearman +0.377, monotonic across quartiles.
- **RaSP~Rosetta only в‰€ 0.61** (NOT near-redundant as В§9's one-physics-axis handoff assumes) вЂ”
  candidate cause: data-gen Rosetta (WSL PyRosetta) may run a different protocol than the Rosetta RaSP
  approximates. To investigate.
- **DynaMut2 most differentiated** (0.31вЂ“0.48 with others) вЂ” validates the dynamics-axis
  independence claim.
- **Property axes orthogonal** (CamSol в€’0.15, ESM в€’0.13 to exp).
- **Destabilizing bias** is real, systematic, regime-localized to the stabilizing tail, and largely a
  per-voter constant offset (RaSP +0.45 slope в‰€ 0.93; ThermoMPNN +0.57 with slope-compression
  в‰€ 0.63). Removing the offset alone nearly restores each voter's stabilizing-tail median to
  experiment в†’ the bias is knowable as per-voter metadata. Matters most for engineering (stabilizer
  hunting lives on that tail).

**Multi-cycle cartesian_ddg diagnostic вЂ” вњ… COMPLETE (2026-06-12); attended DECISION: PROTOCOL STAYS TORSION.**
CC ran cartesian at **3 AND 5 cycles** on **24 mutations** вЂ” **2LZM 9** (Ssym_dir, classical denaturation
anchor) / **2WQG 9** / **2HBB 6** (S669) вЂ” on the benchmark-correct structures (set-keyed manifest
resolution, wt-verified), apples-to-apples vs the existing cart-1 / torsion / exp in
`benchmark_rows.jsonl`. **24/24 scored, 0 not_computed**; scratch/gitignored artifacts
(`cart_diag_cyc{3,5}.jsonl`); `benchmark_rows.jsonl` untouched.
**FRAMING CAVEAT (record first):** on this CLEAN subset the 1-cycle arm was **NOT broken** (cart-1
pooled r 0.44, 2LZM r 0.56, RMSE ~2вЂ“3, bias ~в€’0.5) вЂ” unlike the global benchmark's broken arm
(r в€’0.01, RMSE 11, bias ~в€’4). The global breakage was driven by larger/clash-prone proteins (the
+97 REU tail) **NOT in this subset**. So this characterizes **refinement on CLEAN folds, NOT rescue of
the globally-broken arm вЂ” the hard proteins were not tested.**
**Findings (descriptive):** **Q1 Refinement (vs exp):** on 2LZM r improves monotonically
**0.556 в†’ 0.736 в†’ 0.781** (1в†’3в†’5), cart-5 RMSE 2.44 lowest, and cart-5 **beats torsion** (r 0.781 vs
0.611; RMSE 2.44 vs 3.91) вЂ” real ranking signal on the clean anchor; BUT median bias is
cycle-dependent and does NOT clean up (в€’0.59 в†’ в€’1.55 в†’ +0.50). On the mini-proteins more cycles did
**NOT** help (RMSE rises with cycles; 2HBB r non-monotone). **Q2 Convergence (exp-independent): NOT
settled by 5** вЂ” cart5~cart3 r ~0.5 (2LZM 0.516, pooled 0.535), mean per-mut |О”| ~3 REU (max 6.8) вЂ”
still in substantial motion at 5. **Stabilizers (3 classical 2LZM, directional only):** swing wildly
with cycle count вЂ” K16E (exp в€’0.50): в€’4.21 в†’ в€’2.05 в†’ +0.87 (flips destabilizing at 5); T157R (в€’0.30):
в€’0.58 в†’ в€’1.88 в†’ в€’5.57; V131M (в€’0.10): в€’0.21 в†’ в€’3.79 в†’ +0.12 вЂ” no cycle count reliably captures the
tail. **cart-vs-torsion agreement (exp-independent):** moderate, protein-dependent (~0.54 pooled) вЂ”
correlated but genuinely distinct protocols.
**DECISION (attended вЂ” Claude + user): PROTOCOL STAYS TORSION; multi-cycle cartesian does NOT earn the
switch.** Reasons recorded: (1) **non-convergence at 5 cycles** is disqualifying for a production
default (values still moving ~3 REU, 3в†”5 r ~0.5 вЂ” "5 cycles" is a moving target); (2) magnitude/bias
is cycle-dependent в†’ not even a fixed offset correction applies; (3) **no generalization** вЂ” the
mini-proteins don't refine; (4) the **stabilizer tail** (engineering-critical) is unstable at every
cycle count; (5) **tens-of-times the cost** of torsion (~73вЂ“115 s/mut vs ~2.7 s). The 2LZM rank gain
is real but **thin (n=9, one protein)** and doesn't justify the switch. **REINFORCES** the benchmark's
`protocol=torsion` call (В§7).
**RESIDUAL NICHE (a maybe, not a commitment):** cartesian could be an optional future deep *ranking*
tool on a shortlist of well-folded candidates вЂ” **only if the convergence problem is solved first**.
Revisit-later, not adopted now.
**DEPRIORITIZED FOLLOW-UPS (optional; the torsion call is stable without them):** extend cycles
(cart-8/10, to find where it settles) and widen to the **HARD** proteins (to test whether multi-cycle
rescues the cases that actually broke). The reusable driver is parked on branch
`tooling/cart-cycle-diagnostic` (off main, not merged). Ties to the Backlog "adopt canonical
cartesian_ddg" item.

**Future robustness queue (updated 2026-06-11).** вњ… Anti-symmetry at scale **DONE** (349/352 Ssym
pairs reconstructed + validated, В§7). Still open: **DynaMut2 clean-provenance eval** (this benchmark
could not validate it вЂ” all rows training/unknown, S669-only, n=42; accuracy unverified); RaSP-vs-
deployed-Rosetta protocol check; out-of-distribution proteins (does the calibration transfer?);
DynaMut2 mm-sign live reconfirmation (lift `DYNAMUT2_MM_SIGN_VERIFIED` only when the endpoint recovers
and the mm sign battery converges вЂ” **unaffected by this benchmark**, single-mutant sign confirmed but
mm path untested).

---

### Standalone Sequence Viewer/Editor вЂ” MVP BUILT (landed 2026-06-10)

> **вњ… MVP BUILT / landed (2026-06-10).** The project's **first standalone GUI surface** вЂ” `seq_editor/`
> (PySide6, main venv; `python -m seq_editor`). MVP slice live-verified against ChimeraX (read+display
> w/ gap-aware numbering, clickв†’3D select, on-command reverse-sync, substitutionв†’variant, async fold).
> Growth-arc items below remain DEFERRED. Parallel track to the stability exporter/aggregate.

**What.** A separate-window amino-acid sequence viewer/editor (CLC Main Workbench-style) linked to the
ChimeraX structure viewer вЂ” displays the loaded models' sequences, residues selectable + editable, with
WT-vs-iteration alignment and one-click fold (ColabFold) of edited sequences. **Distinct from
`sequence_viewer.py`** (which integrates ChimeraX's BUILT-IN Sequence Viewer); this is an EXTERNAL
StructureBot-owned window.

**Why external (not the built-in viewer).** The built-in viewer can't edit sequences, manage
WT/iteration variants, or launch folds. **TRADE-OFF (explicit):** the built-in viewer gets real-time
bidirectional 3Dв†”sequence linkage natively; an external window re-implements that over REST and gives
up the free native sync (see sync model). The external editor is a different tool (editor + variant/
iteration manager + fold launcher), **not** a replacement for the built-in viewer's annotation/coloring
role.

**Reuses (most of the data spine already exists).**
- Sequences/chains/resnums over REST + gap-aware numbering + resnumв†”position: `sequence_viewer.py`,
  `proteinmpnn_bridge.chain_resnum_to_seqpos`.
- WT-vs-iteration alignment: `proteinmpnn_bridge.build_alignment_fasta` (ungapped 1:1 today; generalize
  for iterations).
- Selection read/parse over REST, source-agnostic: `selection.py` (`read_selection`, `Selection`).
- Fold an edited sequence: `colabfold_bridge.py` (complete; MPNNв†’ColabFold auto-pull already wired at
  the router).
- Substitution = mutation: existing `swapaa` / mutation machinery.

**New (the actual build).**
- **GUI layer** вЂ” StructureBot's FIRST standalone GUI surface (so far: REPL/chat + ChimeraX windows +
  Rich console; no custom GUI event loop). TOOLKIT = a foundation decision (PySide6/PyQt native vs local
  web UI вЂ” see below).
- **Reverse sync (ChimeraXв†’window)** вЂ” the main cost-center. REST is request-response, no event push;
  the project is poll-on-command (no background polling). MVP syncs the window from ChimeraX selection
  **ON COMMAND/REFRESH** (consistent with the existing design), NOT real-time. Real-time later via a
  polling timer (departs from no-background-polling) OR a ChimeraX-side bundle hooking the
  `selection changed` trigger (event-driven, adds a ChimeraX-side component). Viewerв†’ChimeraX (push a
  `select` command) is free either way.
- **Edit semantics вЂ” split:** substitution (A30V) в†’ maps to a mutation (`swapaa` / variant track),
  easy. Insertion/deletion в†’ changes length, breaks resnum alignment, no structural equivalent в†’ a
  sequence-level VARIANT decoupled from the loaded structure, resolved by re-folding (ColabFold). The
  editв†’fold loop is the coherent home for indels.

**MVP slice (scaffold first):** standalone window в†’ pull loaded models' sequences (reuse) в†’ click
residue в†’ select in 3D (push) в†’ reverse-sync on command/refresh (not real-time) в†’ apply a substitution
в†’ fold the edited sequence via the existing ColabFold path. **DEFER:** real-time reverse sync, indel
editing, full alignment/iteration manager.

**Growth arc:** real-time bidirectional sync (timer or ChimeraX bundle); indel editing + variant/
iteration management; WT-vs-iterations alignment view; exportable iterations; richer CLC-like editing +
coloring parity.

**Discipline:** error-first (a sync/fold failure degrades, never crashes the window or the REPL);
lossless (variants tracked, never overwritten); reuse the existing sequence/numbering/alignment spine
(don't re-implement resnum mapping); probe-before-build (verify the toolkit + REST reads against a live
model in the MVP smoke). В§0 Intent/Render doesn't apply (GUI, not an LLM-translation op).

**Status:** MVP BUILT / landed (2026-06-10) вЂ” `seq_editor/` (controller + PySide6 view + entry
point + 12 controller tests); live-verified. Growth-arc items above remain DEFERRED.

## 12. Session Continuity Notes

**For starting a new co-pilot conversation:**

- **Test count (2026-05-31)**: 535 collected, **523 passing** (12 benchmark tests skip without WSL2+PyRosetta). Non-benchmark suite runs in ~36s (`pytest tests/ --ignore=tests/test_rosetta_benchmark.py -q`). Only pre-existing BioPython `RuntimeWarning`s; no unknown-marker warnings.
- **Last built/validated this session**: (1) double-mutant bridge validated **live end-to-end**; (2) **session auto-restore** on startup + `clear session` command (`session_state.try_load`, `main._maybe_restore_session`); (3) **ChimeraX auto-reconnect** on dropped REST connection; (4) **DynaMut2 single-parser fix** (status-based API) + `ddg_source` provenance + `relax_cycles` param + Ubuntu-24.04 corrections in `rosetta_bridge.py`; (5) **PyRosetta ddG standalone validation** (1HSG controls, T4/2LZM cross-check, aggregation + convergence diagnostics). All session work is committed; working tree clean.
- **Convergence diagnostic COMPLETE** (2026-05-29): large-cavity bias is **partially convergence-fixable** вЂ” more relax cycles move every median toward experiment and shrink spread (7.61в†’5.13 kcal/mol), but at 8+8 only ~half the gap closes. `rosetta_bridge.py` is now **free** (no PyRosetta running).
- **Multi-trajectory ddG + 2LZM confirmation COMPLETE** (2026-05-30): the tiered `validate_ddg` shipped and the full 2LZM panel was scored at the validation tier (N=5 Г— 8+8, median): **RMSE 2.73, MAE 2.59, r +0.50, sign 90% вЂ” all revised thresholds (r>0.3, RMSE<4.0, sign>=60%) PASS**. RMSE/MAE roughly halve vs single-trajectory while r is unchanged (gain in magnitude, not ranking). Build-queue item 1 is fully closed.
- **Crystal-water fix + benchmark thresholds DONE (2026-05-30)**: `ROSETTA_STRIP_WATERS` flag + preserve code path (commit 3318bc9) re-append crystallographic HOH; validated on Barnase T26A (strip в€’0.34 wrong-sign в†’ preserve +3.47 correct, +3.80 shift, 216 HOH). Benchmark thresholds relaxed to r>0.3/RMSE<4.0/sign>=60% (commit db3add2).
- **Water-handling default RESOLVED (2026-05-31)**: `ROSETTA_STRIP_WATERS` default **reverted to `True` (strip)** вЂ” the validated, standard-Rosetta-practice baseline; preserve-all-static is a documented anti-pattern and only the strip path is panel-validated. **Preserve is opt-in** (`ROSETTA_STRIP_WATERS=false`), validated only on buried-water T26A. The committed 2LZM panel numbers (RMSE 2.73, r +0.50, sign 90%) therefore again describe the **default** path. The real future fix is **selective buried-only / movable** waters (Build Queue В§9); preserve-path 2LZM re-validation is downgraded to *conditional* (only if preserve is promoted to default or made selective).
- **Benchmark-test honesty DONE (2026-05-31)**: `test_rosetta_benchmark.py` re-scoped (Build Queue В§9 item closed). (a) cp1252 `UnicodeEncodeError` fixed вЂ” the `вњ“`/`вњ—` summary glyph is now ASCII `[PASS]`/`[FAIL]`, plus a best-effort UTF-8 stream reconfigure in `compute_benchmark_correlation` (same pattern as `validate_2lzm_panel.py`). (b) per-mutation tests no longer gate on noise: the В±2.0 kcal/mol magnitude asserts are **gone**, sign is asserted **only** for `|experimental| > 1.5` (`SIGN_ASSERT_MIN_ABS_EXP` + `_check_sign` helper) and near-neutral mutations are **recorded but not asserted**; every per-mutation test still writes to `benchmark_results.json`. (c) `test_benchmark_correlation_acceptable` is now THE gate (r>0.3 / RMSE<4.0 / signв‰Ґ60%) with a `MIN_BENCHMARK_ENTRIES=6` minimum-N guard that **skips, not fails**, below the floor. Verified: non-benchmark suite **523 passed**; benchmark module collects 12 + **skips all 12 cleanly** when WSL2/PyRosetta absent (simulated by forcing `wsl_bridge._WSL_AVAILABLE_CACHE=False`); cp1252 + logic exercised offline with synthetic data. **Did NOT run the hours-long live benchmark** (on this dev machine PyRosetta IS available, so a bare `pytest tests/test_rosetta_benchmark.py` would execute it live вЂ” guard accordingly). **Immediate next is now features**: ColabFold в†’ RFdiffusion. *(Update: ColabFold env now stood up вЂ” see the ColabFold env bullet below; the `venv310` plan was superseded by a WSL2 Py-3.12 env.)*
- **Benchmark-honesty follow-up DONE (2026-05-31, recovered after a machine crash; committed after 06f6478)**: two further `test_rosetta_benchmark.py` fixes. **Fix A** вЂ” buried В§8-failure-mode-2 wrong-sign mutations under the default strip-water path (**G88V, V82A**) are `xfail(strict=False, raises=AssertionError)`; T26A is bucket-1 (record-only, `|exp|=1.3`). **Fix B** вЂ” `STRUCTUREBOT_RUN_LIVE_BENCHMARK=1` opt-in gate (`run live iff opt-in AND WSL2 AND PyRosetta`, short-circuit) so the hours-long live suite never auto-fires on this PyRosetta-equipped dev box. Verified offline: non-benchmark **523 passed**; `pytest tests/test_rosetta_benchmark.py` в†’ **12 skipped, 0 run, 0.04s**. **To run the live benchmark you must now explicitly set `STRUCTUREBOT_RUN_LIVE_BENCHMARK=1`** (a bare invocation no longer runs it).
- **Throwaway diagnostics (safe to delete, never commit)**: `ddg_audit.md` and `validate_2lzm_run.log` in the repo root are one-off diagnostic scratch from this session вЂ” delete freely. `scripts/validate_2lzm_results.json` is **validation data** (the authoritative 2LZM panel numbers; gitignored) вЂ” **keep it**. None of these three should be committed.
- **PyRosetta ddG status**: works for **ranking + sign** (T4/2LZM: r=+0.487 single-traj, +0.499 validation tier; sign 90вЂ“100%) and the validation tier now **roughly halves magnitude error** (RMSE 5.2в†’2.73). Aggregate by **median** (min refuted). Absolute ddG is tighter but still **approximate (~В±2.7 kcal/mol)**.
- **ColabFold ENVIRONMENT DONE (2026-05-31, `feat/colabfold-env`)** вЂ” env stand-up + GPU validation only; **the bridge (`colabfold_bridge.py`) is the NEXT task, deliberately not built here**. Isolated WSL2 **Python-3.12** venv `~/colabfold_env` (the old "venv310 shared with RFdiffusion" plan is **superseded**). Hermetic CUDA via pip. **Exact installed versions**: python **3.12.3**, colabfold **1.6.1**, alphafold-colabfold **2.3.13**, dm-haiku **0.0.16**, jax **0.5.3**, jaxlib **0.5.3**, jax-cuda12-plugin/pjrt **0.5.3**, nvidia-cuda-nvcc-cu12 **12.9.86**, cuDNN **9.23.0.39**. WSL2 driver **596.49 / CUDA 13.2**, RTX 5070 Ti. **GPU+sm_120 verified** (2048Ві matmul, no ptxas error). **Reconciliation gotcha**: `jax[cuda12]` latest (0.10.1) works on sm_120 but ColabFold caps `jax<0.6.0` в†’ 0.5.3; you MUST realign the cuda plugin (`pip install "jax[cuda12]==0.5.3"`) or the PJRT C-API aborts. **Smoke fold** (villin HP36, remote MSA server, GPU, 1 model/1 recycle): **rank_001 pLDDT 82.4, pTM 0.44**, output `~/colabfold_test/out/`, wall 13:59 (mostly one-time 3.47 GB weight download + first sm_120 XLA compile). **RFdiffusion stays a SEPARATE env** вЂ” do not couple. `pyrosetta_env` untouched.
- **ColabFold BRIDGE v1 DONE (2026-05-31, `feat/colabfold-bridge`)** вЂ” standalone `colabfold_bridge.py` (Option A) wraps the env from `feat/colabfold-env`. `ColabFoldBridge.predict(sequence, copies, template, num_models, num_recycle, quick)` runs an f-string worker via `wsl_bridge.COLABFOLD_PYTHON` (remote MSA, no local DBs), returns ranked PDB + mean/per-residue pLDDT + PAE + pTM(/ipTM) + PNG paths, **input-hash cache** `cache/colabfold_{hash}/`. **Total-residue guard** `COLABFOLD_MAX_TOTAL_RESIDUES` (default 1500): over budget в†’ no launch + clear OOM-risk message; runtime CUDA-OOM also caught. Router: explicit intent (`colabfold`/`alphafold`/"fold вЂ¦ as a `<oligomer>`"/template-fold) parses copies+template+quick+sequence, dispatches `_run_colabfold`, stores trimmed result in `session_state.colabfold_results`. **Viz**: open ranked PDB в†’ `color byattribute bfactor вЂ¦ palette alphafold` (native pLDDT) в†’ `sequence chain` в†’ optional `matchmaker` vs compare_to (default = loaded primary model); model id from `session.next_model_id()` (matches main's open tracking); PAE/pLDDT/coverage PNGs auto-open in the OS viewer. New `CHIMERAX_SHOW_SEQUENCE_ON_OPEN` flag opens the Sequence Viewer for ALL structure opens (chimerax_bridge.run_commands, fire-and-forget). `_ElapsedTicker` extended with an approximate ETA. **Tests: 33** in `tests/test_colabfold_bridge.py` (all mocked); full non-benchmark suite **556 passed + 1 skipped**. **Optional live monomer fold RAN** through the real bridge (opt-in `STRUCTUREBOT_RUN_LIVE_COLABFOLD=1`): villin HP36, GPU confirmed, **mean pLDDT 82.4, pTM 0.44**, 616 s вЂ” validated the worker's real ColabFold-1.6.1 output-dir globs + scores-JSON parsing. **DEFERRED** (next): fused validate-design meta-tool, MPNN-result sequence auto-pull, batch top-N, amber relax, single_sequence, generalized ETA. **Multimer caveat**: budget guard provisional; large homo-tetramers expected to OOM в†’ remote/alternate-GPU handoff is backlog.

| 2026-06-01 | 645 (626вњ“/19s) | fix(translator): **stop over-eager "flagged by the API safety filter" rejections of benign design requests** (`fix/translator-false-refusals`). Mechanism = (b): not StructureBot's own filter вЂ” `translator._call_api` raised `RefusalError` whenever the Claude translation call returned empty `content`, and `main._handle_request` framed ANY such case as a safety filter with an opaque, epitope-specific rephrasing hint and NO retry. So a single transient/over-eager empty response (e.g. on "redesign the dimer interface residues to be hydrophilic, no cysteines") blocked the request, while a near-identical phrasing passed. Fixes: (1) **one automatic retry** in `_call_api` вЂ” re-issuing the identical request typically succeeds, since the decline is non-deterministic; (2) **system-prompt SCOPE framing** in `_STATIC_SYSTEM` вЂ” routine protein-engineering (interface/dimer redesign, hydrophilic/charged substitutions, excluding/introducing cysteines, stabilising mutations, epitope mapping) is declared STANDARD structural biology that must be translated, not declined; (3) **transparent message** вЂ” on a genuine decline (after retry) the real `stop_reason` is surfaced via `_report_translation_decline`, not a generic "safety filter" assumption (main.py now catches `RefusalError` by type + the legacy message pattern). Tests: +3 in `tests/test_translator.py` (the benign request is NOT flagged вЂ” retry rescues it; `_call_api` retries exactly once then raises a transparent `RefusalError` with the real stop_reason and no "safety filter"; the prompt frames routine design as legitimate). All surfaced in the evidence-rich report + `session_state.validate_design_results`; still no binary verdict. **Tests**: `test_validate_design.py` 27в†’34 вЂ” regression test updated to assert all-pairs headline (pruned still captured); new parse/fallback, concentration math+descriptor, top-K, Kabsch-localizes-displaced-residue, colour-command tests.
